NodeId\n81\t                    let new_node_id = crate::topology::NodeId::new(state.new_node.0.clone());\n82\t\n83\t                    // Only add if not already in targets\n84\t                    if !targets.contains(&new_node_id) {\n85\t                        targets.push(new_node_id);\n86\t                    }\n87\t                }\n88\t            }\n89\t        }\n90\t    }\n91\t\n92\t    targets\n93\t}\n94\t\n95\t/// Select the replica group for a query (round-robin by query counter).\n96\t///\n97\t/// Returns 0 when there are no replica groups (caller handles the empty case).\n98\tpub fn query_group(query_seq: u64, replica_groups: u32) -> u32 {\n99\t    if replica_groups == 0 {\n100\t        return 0;\n101\t    }\n102\t    (query_seq % replica_groups as u64) as u32\n103\t}\n104\t\n105\t/// The covering set for a search: one node per shard within the chosen group.\n106\tpub fn covering_set(shard_count: u32, group: &Group, rf: usize, query_seq: u64) -> Vec<NodeId> {\n107\t    (0..shard_count)\n108\t        .map(|shard_id| {\n109\t            let replicas = assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, group.nodes(), rf);\n110\t            // rotate through replicas for intra-group load balancing\n111\t            replicas[(query_seq as usize) % replicas.len()].clone()\n112\t        })\n113\t        .collect::<HashSet<_>>()\n114\t        .into_iter()\n115\t        .collect()\n116\t}\n117\t\n118\t/// Covering set with settings version floor filtering (plan §13.5).\n119\t///\n120\t/// Excludes nodes whose settings version for the given index is below `floor`.\n121\t/// Returns None if no covering set can be assembled (caller should return 503).\n122\tpub fn covering_set_with_version_floor(\n123\t    shard_count: u32,\n124\t    group: &Group,\n125\t    rf: usize,\n126\t    query_seq: u64,\n127\t    index: &str,\n128\t    floor: u64,\n129\t    version_checker: &impl Fn(&str, &str) -> u64,\n130\t) -> Option<Vec<NodeId>> {\n131\t    let mut result = Vec::new();\n132\t    let mut used_nodes = HashSet::new();\n133\t\n134\t    for shard_id in 0..shard_count {\n135\t        let replicas = assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, group.nodes(), rf);\n136\t\n137\t        // Filter replicas by settings version floor, then by query_seq rotation\n138\t        let eligible: Vec<_> = replicas\n139\t            .iter()\n140\t            .filter(|node_id| {\n141\t                let version = version_checker(index, node_id.as_str());\n142\t                version >= floor\n143\t            })\n144\t            .collect();\n145\t\n146\t        if eligible.is_empty() {\n147\t            // No eligible replica for this shard\n148\t            return None;\n149\t        }\n150\t\n151\t        // Rotate through eligible replicas using query_seq\n152\t        let selected = eligible[query_seq as usize % eligible.len()];\n153\t        if used_nodes.insert(selected.clone()) {\n154\t            result.push(selected.clone());\n155\t        }\n156\t    }\n157\t\n158\t    Some(result)\n159\t}\n160\t\n161\t/// Compute the shard ID for a document's primary key.\n162\tpub fn shard_for_key(primary_key: &str, shard_count: u32) -> u32 {\n163\t    let mut h = XxHash64::with_seed(0);\n164\t    primary_key.hash(&mut h);\n165\t    (h.finish() % shard_count as u64) as u32\n166\t}\n167\t\n168\t/// Count differences between two shard assignments.\n169\t///\n170\t/// Returns the number of shard-node pairs that differ between old and new.\n171\t/// For each shard, counts nodes in new assignment that weren't in old.\n172\tpub fn count_assignment_diff(\n173\t    old_shards: &[(u32, Vec<NodeId>)],\n174\t    new_shards: &[(u32, Vec<NodeId>)],\n175\t) -> usize {\n176\t    let old_map: std::collections::HashMap<_, _> = old_shards\n177\t        .iter()\n178\t        .map(|(shard, nodes)| (*shard, nodes.clone()))\n179\t        .collect();\n180\t\n181\t    let mut diff = 0;\n182\t    for (shard, new_nodes) in new_shards {\n183\t        if let Some(old_nodes) = old_map.get(shard) {\n184\t            // Count nodes in new that weren't in old (counts each change once)\n185\t            for node in new_nodes {\n186\t                if !old_nodes.contains(node) {\n187\t                    diff += 1;\n188\t                }\n189\t            }\n190\t        }\n191\t    }\n192\t    diff\n193\t}\n194\t\n195\t#[cfg(test)]\n196\tmod tests {\n197\t    use super::*;\n198\t    use crate::topology::{Node, NodeId};\n199\t    use     for i in 0u32..6 {\n567\t            let rg = if i < 3 { 0 } else { 1 };\n568\t            let node = Node::new(\n569\t                NodeId::new(format!(\"node-{i}\")),\n570\t P1.3-A6: query_group distribution is uniform (chi-square test).\n595\t    #[test]\n596\t    fn test_query_group_uniform_distribution() {\n597\t        let replica_groups = 5u32;\n598\t        let samples = 10_000;\n599\t\n600\t        let mut counts = vec![0usize; replica_groups as usize];\n601\t        for query_seq in 0..samples {\n602\t            let g = query_group(query_seq as u64, replica_groups);\n603\t            counts[g as usize] += 1;\n604\t        }\n605\t\n606\t        // Expected count per group: samples / RG\n607\t        let expected = samples as f64 / replica_groups as f64;\n608\t\n609\t        // Chi-square statistic: sum((observed - expected)^2 / expected)\n610\t        let chi_square: f64 = counts\n611\t            .iter()\n612\t            .map(|&observed| {\n613\t                let diff = observed as f64 - expected;\n614\t                (diff * diff) / expected\n615\t            })\n616\t            .sum();\n617\t\n618\t        // Degrees of freedom = RG - 1 = 4\n619\t        // Critical value at p=0.95 is ~9.49\n620\t        let critical_value = 9.49;\n621\t\n622\t        assert!(\n623\t            chi_square < critical_value,\n624\t            \"query_group distribution not uniform: chi-square={} > {}\",\n625\t            chi_square,\n626\t            critical_value\n627\t        );\n628\t    }\n629\t\n630\t    /// P1.3-A7: covering_set Rendezvous hash-based routing and shard assignment.\n\nuse crate::migration::{MigrationCoordinator, ShardId};\nuse crate::topology::{Group, NodeId, Topology};\nuse std::collections::HashSet;\nuse std::hash::{Hash, Hasher};\nuse twox_hash::XxHash64;\n\n/// Compute a rendezvous score for a shard+node pair.\n///\n/// Higher scores win; used for deterministic shard assignment.\npub fn score(shard_id: u32, node_id: &str) -> u64 {\n    let mut h = XxHash64::with_seed(0);\n    shard_id.hash(&mut h);\n    node_id.hash(&mut h);\n    h.finish()\n}\n\n/// Assign a shard to `rf` nodes within a single replica group.\n///\n/// `group_nodes` is the subset of nodes belonging to that group.\n///\n/// Sorts by score descending, breaking ties lexicographically on node_id\n/// for deterministic resolution.\npub fn assign_shard_in_group(shard_id: u32, group_nodes: &[NodeId], rf: usize) -> Vec<NodeId> {\n    let mut scored: Vec<(u64, &NodeId)> = group_nodes\n        .iter()\n        .map(|n| (score(shard_id, n.as_str()), n))\n        .collect();\n    scored.sort_unstable_by(|a, b| {\n        b.0.cmp(&a.0)\n            .then_with(|| a.1.as_str().cmp(b.1.as_str()))\n    });\n    scored\n        .into_iter()\n        .take(rf)\n        .map(|(_, n)| n.clone())\n        .collect()\n}\n\n/// All write targets for a document: the RF nodes in EACH replica group.\npub fn write_targets(shard_id: u32, topology: &Topology) -> Vec<NodeId> {\n    topology\n        .groups()\n        .flat_map(|group| assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, group.nodes(), topology.rf()))\n        .collect()\n}\n\n/// All write targets for a document, considering dual-write state during migration.\n///\n/// This is the migration-aware version of `write_targets`. When a shard is in\n/// dual-write phase (node addition in progress), it includes both the old owner\n/// AND the new node in the target list to ensure no writes are lost during migration.\n///\n/// # Arguments\n/// * `shard_id` - The shard ID being written to\n/// * `topology` - The cluster topology\n/// * `migration_coordinator` - Optional migration coordinator for dual-write detection\n///\n/// # Returns\n/// A vector of node IDs that should receive the write. During dual-write for a shard,\n/// this includes both the standard RF nodes AND the new node.\npub fn write_targets_with_migration(\n    shard_id: u32,\n    topology: &Topology,\n    migration_coordinator: Option<&MigrationCoordinator>,\n) -> Vec<NodeId> {\n    let shard = ShardId(shard_id);\n\n    // Start with standard write targets\n    let mut targets: Vec<NodeId> = write_targets(shard_id, topology);\n\n    // Check if this shard is in dual-write phase\n    if let Some(coordinator) = migration_coordinator {\n        if coordinator.is_dual_write_active(shard) {\n            // Find migrations affecting this shard\n            for (_mid, state) in coordinator.get_all_migrations() {\n                if state.affected_shards.contains_key(&shard) {\n                    // This shard is being migrated - include the new node\n                    // Convert migration NodeId to topology NodeId\n                    let new_node_id = crate::topology::NodeId::new(state.new_node.0.clone());\n\n                    // Only add if not already in targets\n                    if !targets.contains(&new_node_id) {\n                        targets.push(new_node_id);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    targets\n}\n\n/// Select the replica group for a query (round-robin by query counter).\n///\n/// Returns 0 when there are no replica groups (caller handles the empty case).\npub fn query_group(query_seq: u64, replica_groups: u32) -> u32 {\n    if replica_groups == 0 {\n        return 0;\n    }\n    (query_seq % replica_groups as u64) as u32\n}\n\n/// The covering set for a search: one node per shard within the chosen group.\npub fn covering_set(shard_count: u32, group: &Group, rf: usize, query_seq: u64) -> Vec<NodeId> {\n    (0..shard_count)\n        .map(|shard_id| {\n            let replicas = assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, group.nodes(), rf);\n            // rotate through replicas for intra-group load balancing\n            replicas[(query_seq as usize) % replicas.len()].clone()\n        })\n        .collect::<HashSet<_>>()\n        .into_iter()\n        .collect()\n}\n\n/// Covering set with settings version floor filtering (plan §13.5).\n///\n/// Excludes nodes whose settings version for the given index is below `floor`.\n/// Returns None if no covering set can be assembled (caller should return 503).\npub fn covering_set_with_version_floor(\n    shard_count: u32,\n    group: &Group,\n    rf: usize,\n    query_seq: u64,\n    index: &str,\n    floor: u64,\n    version_checker: &impl Fn(&str, &str) -> u64,\n) -> Option<Vec<NodeId>> {\n    let mut result = Vec::new();\n    let mut used_nodes = HashSet::new();\n\n    for shard_id in 0..shard_count {\n        let replicas = assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, group.nodes(), rf);\n\n        // Filter replicas by settings version floor, then by query_seq rotation\n        let eligible: Vec<_> = replicas\n            .iter()\n            .filter(|node_id| {\n                let version = version_checker(index, node_id.as_str());\n                version >= floor\n            })\n            .collect();\n\n        if eligible.is_empty() {\n            // No eligible replica for this shard\n            return None;\n        }\n\n        // Rotate through eligible replicas using query_seq\n        let selected = eligible[query_seq as usize % eligible.len()];\n        if used_nodes.insert(selected.clone()) {\n            result.push(selected.clone());\n        }\n    }\n\n    Some(result)\n}\n\n/// Compute the shard ID for a document's primary key.\npub fn shard_for_key(primary_key: &str, shard_count: u32) -> u32 {\n    let mut h = XxHash64::with_seed(0);\n    primary_key.hash(&mut h);\n    (h.finish() % shard_count as u64) as u32\n}\n\n/// Count differences between two shard assignments.\n///\n/// Returns the number of shard-node pairs that differ between old and new.\n/// For each shard, counts nodes in new assignment that weren't in old.\npub fn count_assignment_diff(\n    old_shards: &[(u32, Vec<NodeId>)],\n    new_shards: &[(u32, Vec<NodeId>)],\n) -> usize {\n    let old_map: std::collections::HashMap<_, _> = old_shards\n        .iter()\n        .map(|(shard, nodes)| (*shard, nodes.clone()))\n        .collect();\n\n    let mut diff = 0;\n    for (shard, new_nodes) in new_shards {\n        if let Some(old_nodes) = old_map.get(shard) {\n            // Count nodes in new that weren't in old (counts each change once)\n            for node in new_nodes {\n                if !old_nodes.contains(node) {\n                    diff += 1;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    diff\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use uniform (chi-square test).\n    #[test]\n    fn test_query_group_uniform_distribution() {\n        let replica_groups = 5u32;\n        let samples = 10_000;\n\n        let mut counts = vec![0usize; replica_groups as usize];\n        for query_seq in 0..samples {\n            let g = query_group(query_seq as u64, replica_groups);\n            counts[g as usize] += 1;\n        }\n\n        // Expected count per group: samples / RG\n        let expected = samples as f64 / replica_groups as f64;\n\n        // Chi-square statistic: sum((observed - expected)^2 / expected)\n        let chi_square: f64 = counts\n            .iter()\n            .map(|&observed| {\n                let diff = observed as f64 - expected;\n                (diff * diff) / expected\n            })\n            .sum();\n\n        // Degrees of freedom = RG - 1 = 4\n        // Critical value at p=0.95 is ~9.49\n        let critical_value = 9.49;\n\n        assert!(\n            chi_square < critical_value,\n            \"query_group distribution not uniform: chi-square={} > {}\",\n            chi_square,\n            critical_value\n        );\n    }\n\n    /// P1.3-A7: covering_set rotates replicas by query_seq.\n    #[test]\n    fn test_covering_set_rotates_replicas() {\n        let mut topo = Topology::new(8, 1, 3);\n        for i in 0u32..4 {\n            topo.add_node(Node::new(\n                NodeId::new(format!(\"node-{i}\")),\n                format!(\"http://node-{i}:7700\"),\n                0,\n            ));\n        }\n\n        let group = match self.rrf_score.partial_cmp(&other.rrf_score) {\n169\t            Some(Ordering::Equal) => {\n170\t                // Secondary sort: primary key ascending for deterministic tie-breaking\n171\t .and_then(|v| v.as_str())\n251\t                        .unwrap_or(\"\")\n252\t                        .to_string();\n253\t\n254\t                    // RRF contribution: 1 / (k + rank + 1)\n255\t Entry::Vacant(e) => {\n262\t                            e.insert(RRFDocument {\n263\t                                rrf_score: rrf_contribution,\n264\t                       // Document appears in multiple shards: sum RRF contributions.\n270\t                            e.get_mut().rrf_score += rrf_contribution;\n271\t                        }\n272\t #[test]\n686\t    fn test_merge_global_sort() {\n687\t        let input = MergeInput {\n688\t            shard_hits: vec![\n689\t                make_shard_response(vec![make_hit(\"doc1\", 0.5, 0)], ],\n693\t            offset: 0,\n694\t            limit: 10,\n695\t            client_requested_score: true,\n696\t            facets: None,\n697\t        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n698\t        };\n699\t\n700\t        let result = merge(input).unwrap();\n701\t        assert_eq!(result.hits.len(), 3);\n702\t\n703\t        // RRF: all docs are at rank 0 in their respective shards.\n704\t rank (lower position) contributes more to RRF score.\n713\t        // shard0: [low_rank_doc (rank 0), mid_rank_doc (rank 10)]\n714\t        // shard1: [high_rank_doc (rank 0)]\n715\t        // shard2: [mid_rank_doc (rank 0) - same doc appears in two shards!]\n716\t        //\n717\t        // Expected RRF scores:\n718\t        // - low_rank_doc: 1/(60+0+1) = 1/61 (only in shard0)\n719\t        // - high_rank_doc: 1/(60+0+1) = 1/61 (only in shard1)\n720\t        // - mid_rank_doc: 1/(60+10+1) + 1/(60+0+1) = 1/71 + 1/61 (rank 10 in shard0, rank 0 in shard2)\n721\t        //\n722\t        // mid_rank_doc should win because it appears in multiple shards.\n723\t\n724\t        let mut shard0_hits = vec![];\n725\t        let mut shard1_hits = vec![];\n726\t        let mut shard2_hits = vec![];\n727\t\n728\t        // Build shard0: low_rank_doc at position 0, mid_rank_doc at position 10\n729\t        shard0_hits.push(make_hit(\"low_rank_doc\", 0.1, 0));\n730\t        for i in 0..9 {\n731\t            shard0_hits.push(make_hit(&format!(\"filler_0_{}\", i), 0.5, 0));\n732\t        }\n733\t        shard0_hits.push(make_hit(\"mid_rank_doc\", 0.2, 0));\n734\t\n735\t        // shard1: high_rank_doc at position 0\n736\t        shard1_hits.push(make_hit(\"high_rank_doc\", 0.3, 1));\n737\t\n738\t        // shard2: mid_rank_doc at position 0 (same doc appears again!)\n739\t        shard2_hits.push(make_hit(\"mid_rank_doc\", 0.4, 2));\n740\t\n741\t        let input = MergeInput {\n742\t            shard_hits: vec![\n743\t                make_shard_response(shard0_hits, 100, 10),\n744\t                make_shard_response(shard1_hits, 100, 10),\n745\t                make_shard_response(shard2_hits, 100, 10),\n746\t            ],\n747\t            offset: 0,\n748\t            limit: 10,\n749\t            client_requested_score: false,\n750\t            facets: None,\n751\t        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n752\t        };\n753\t\n754\t        let result = merge(input).unwrap();\n755\t\n756\t        // mid_rank_doc should be first because it appears in multiple shards\n757\t        // (RRF contributions sum: rank 10 in shard0 + rank 0 in shard2)\n758\t        assert_eq!(result.hits[0].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"mid_rank_doc\");\n759\t\n760\t        // low_rank_doc and high_rank_doc both at rank 0 in their shards\n761\t        // Tie-break by primary key alphabetically\n762\t        assert_eq!(result.hits[1].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"high_rank_doc\");\n763\t        assert_eq!(result.hits[2].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"low_rank_doc\");\n764\t    }\n765\t\n766\t    #[test]\n767\t    fn test_merge_rrf_duplicate_handling() {\n768\t        // Test that the same document appearing in multiple shards\n769\t        // gets its RRF score summed.\n770\t        //\n771\t        // doc1 appears at rank 0 in shard0 and rank 5 in shard1\n772\t        // doc2 appears at rank 0 in shard2\n773\t        //\n774\t        // RRF(doc1) = 1/(60+0+1) + 1/(60+5+1) = 1/61 + 1/66\n775\t        // RRF(doc2) = 1/(60+0+1) = 1/61\n776\t        //\n777\t        // doc1 should rank higher.\n778\t\n779\t        let shard0_hits = vec![make_hit(\"doc1\", 0.1, 0)];\n780\t        let mut shard1_hits = vec![];\n781\t        let shard2_hits = vec![make_hit(\"doc2\", 0.9, 2)];\n782\t\n783\t        // Add filler hits to shard1 to make doc1 appear at rank 5\n784\t        for i in 0..5 {\n785\t            shard1_hits.push(make_hit(&format!(\"filler_1_{}\", i), 0.5, 1));\n786\t        }\n787\t        shard1_hits.push(make_hit(\"doc1\", 0.2, 1));\n788\t\n789\t        let input = MergeInput {\n790\t            shard_hits: vec![\n791\t                make_shard_response(shard0_hits, 50, 10),\n792\t                make_shard_response(shard1_hits, 50, 10),\n793\t                make_shard_response(shard2_hits, 50, 10),\n794\t            ],\n795\t            offset: 0,\n796\t            limit: 10,\n797\t            client_requested_score: false,\n798\t            facets: None,\n799\t        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n800\t        };\n801\t\n802\t        let result = merge(input).unwrap();\n803\t\n804\t        // doc1 should rank higher despite lower score because\n805\t        // it appears in multiple shards and gets RRF contribution boost\n806\t        assert_eq!(result.hits[0].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"doc1\");\n807\t        assert_eq!(result.hits[1].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"doc2\");\n808\t    }\n809\t\n810\t    #[test]\n811\t    fn // Test that RRF ordering is based on rank, not score.\n864\t        // Even though doc3 has highest score, it's ranked lower in its shard.\n865\t        //\n866\t        // shard0: doc2 at rank 0 with score 0.9 (same rank, tie-break by id)\n867\t        // shard1: doc1 at rank 0 with score 0.1 (same rank, tie-break by id)\n868\t        // shard2: doc3 at rank 2 (position 2) with score 1.0 (lower rank)\n869\t        //\n870\t        // RRF scores:\n871\t        // - doc1: 1/61 (rank 0)\n872\t        // - doc2: 1/61 (rank 0)\n873\t        // - filler: 1/62 (rank 1)\n874\t        // - High score, rank 0\n879\t        let shard1_hits = vec![make_hit(\"doc1\", 0.1, 0)]; // Low score, rank 0\n880\t        let shard2_hits = vec![\n881\t            make_hit(\"filler\", 0.5, 2),\n882\t            make_hit(\"filler2\", 0.5, 2),\n883\t            make_hit(\"doc3\", 1.0, 2),  // Highest score, but rank 2\n884\t        ];\n885\t\n886\t        let input = MergeInput {\n887\t            shard_hits: vec![\n888\t                make_shard_response(shard0_hits, 50, 10),\n889\t                make_shard_response(shard1_hits, 50, 10),\n890\t                make_shard_response(shard2_hits, 50, 10),\n891\t            ],\n892\t            offset: 0,\n893\t            limit: 10,\n894\t            client_requested_score: true,\n895\t            facets: None,\n896\t        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n897\t        };\n898\t\n899\t        let result = merge(input).unwrap();\n900\t\n901\t        // doc1 and doc2 both at rank 0, tie-break alphabetically\n902\t assert_eq!(result.hits[2].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"filler\");\n906\t        assert_eq!(result.hits[3].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"filler2\");\n907\t        // doc3 at rank 2, comes last despite highest score\n908\t        assert_eq!(result.hits[4].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"doc3\");\n909\t    }\n910\t\n911\t    #[test]\n912\t    fn test_merge_strips_miroir_fields() {\n913\t        let input = -----------------------------------------------------------------------\n1213\t\n1214\t    #[test]\n1215\t    fn test_rrf_cross_shard_replication_boost() {\n1216\t        // Key RRF property: a document appearing in multiple shards\n1217\t        // gets a higher merged score than a single-shard document,\n1218\t        // even if it ranks lower within each shard.\n1219\t        //\n1220\t        // doc-replicated: rank 5 in shard0, rank 5 in shard1\n1221\t        //   RRF = 1/(60+5+1) + 1/(60+5+1) = 2/66 ≈ 0.0303\n1222\t        // doc-single: rank 0 in shard2\n1223\t        //   RRF = 1/(60+0+1) = 1/61 ≈ 0.0164\n1224\t        //\n1225\t        // doc-replicated should rank higher.\n1226\t\n1227\t        let mut shard0 = vec![];\n1228\t        let mut shard1 = vec![];\n1229\t        for i in 0..5 {\n1230\t            shard0.push(make_hit(&format!(\"filler0-{}\", i), 0.5, 0));\n1231\t            shard1.push(make_hit(&format!(\"filler1-{}\", i), 0.5, 1));\n1232\t        }\n1233\t        shard0.push(make_hit(\"doc-replicated\", 0.1, 0));\n1234\t        shard1.push(make_hit(\"doc-replicated\", 0.1, 1));\n1235\t\n1236\t        let shard2 = vec![make_hit(\"doc-single\", 0.99, 2)];\n1237\t\n1238\t        let strategy = RrfStrategy::default_strategy();\n1239\t        let result = strategy\n1240\t            .merge(MergeInput {\n1241\t                shard_hits: vec![\n1242\t                    make_shard_response(shard0, 100, 10),\n1243\t                    make_shard_response(shard1, 100, 10),\n1244\t                    make_shard_response(shard2, 100, 10),\n1245\t                ],\n1246\t                offset: 0,\n1247\t                limit: 20,\n1248\t                client_requested_score: false,\n1249\t                facets: None,\n1250\t        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n1251\t            })\n1252\t            .unwrap();\n1253\t\n1254\t        let ids: Vec<_> = result.hits.iter().filter_map(|h| h.get(\"id\").and_then(|v| v.as_str())).collect();\n1255\t        let rep_pos = ids.iter().position(|&id| id == \"doc-replicated\").unwrap();\n1256\t        let single_pos = ids.iter().position(|&id| id == \"doc-single\").unwrap();\n1257\t        assert!(\n1258\t            rep_pos < single_pos,\n1259\t            \"Replicated doc at pos {} should rank above single doc at pos {}\",\n1260\t            rep_pos,\n1261\t            single_pos\n1262\t        );\n1263\t    }\n1264\t\n1265\t    #[test]\n1266\t    fn test_rrf_immune_to_score_scale() {\n1267\t        // RRF uses rank only: scores of 0.001 vs 0.999 don't affect preflight.\n1591\t    ///\n1592\t    /// This simulates the scenario described in P12.OP4:\n1593\t    /// - Shard 0 has 1000 docs, term \"rust\" appears in 100 (df=100)\n1594\t    /// - Shard 1 has 100 docs, term \"rust\" appears in 50 (df=50)\n1595\t    ///\n1596\t    /// Without global IDF:\n1597\t    /// - Local IDF(shard 0) = log((1000-100+0.5)/(100+0.5)+1) ≈ 2.2\n1598\t    /// - Local IDF(shard 1) = log((100-50+0.5)/(50+0.5)+1) ≈ 0.7\n1599\t    ///\n1600\t    /// With global IDF:\n1601\t    /// - Global N = 1100, global df = 150\n1602\t    /// - Global IDF = log((1100-150+0.5)/(150+0.5)+1) ≈ 1.8\n1603\t    ///\n1604\t    /// A document with tf=3 for \"rust\" in each shard:\n1605\t    /// - Shard 0 score (local IDF): ~3 * 2.2 = 6.6\n1606\t    /// - Shard 1 score (local IDF): ~3 * 0.7 = 2.1\n1607\t    ///\n1608\t    /// Without global IDF, shard 0 doc ranks higher despite shard 1 having\n1609\t    /// much higher term density (50/100 vs 100/1000).\n1610\t    ///\n1611\t    /// With global IDF, both shards use IDF=1.8, and the doc with higher\n1612\t    /// term density (normalized by document length) ranks correctly.\n1613\t    #[test]\n1614\t    fn test_score_merge_skewed_corpus_integration() {\n1615\t        // Simulate global IDF applied (scores are now comparable)\n1616\t        let strategy = ScoreMergeStrategy::new();\n1617\t\n1618\t        // Doc in large shard with high term frequency but low density\n1619\t        let doc_large_shard = json!({\n1620\t            \"id\": \"doc-large\",\n1621\t            \"title\": \"Rust in Large Shard\",\n1622\t            \"_rankingScore\": 0.75, // After global-IDF normalization\n1623\t        });\n1624\t\n1625\t        // Doc in small shard with lower term frequency but high density\n1626\t        let doc_small_shard = json!({\n1627\t            \"id\": \"doc-small\",\n1628\t            \"title\": \"Rust in Small Shard\",\n1629\t            \"_rankingScore\": 0.85, // After global-IDF normalization\n1630\t        });\n1631\t\n1632\t        // With global IDF, the small shard doc should rank higher\n1633\t        // because its term density is higher (50/100 vs 100/1000)\n1634\t        let input = MergeInput {\n1635\t            shard_hits: vec![\n1636\t                ShardHitPage {\n1637\t                    body: json!({\n1638\t                        \"hits\": [doc_large_shard],\n1639\t                        \"estimatedTotalHits\": 1000,\n1640\t                        \"processingTimeMs\": 10,\n1641\t                    }),\n1642\t                },\n1643\t                ShardHitPage {\n1644\t                    body: json!({\n1645\t                        \"hits\": [doc_small_shard],\n1646\t                        \"estimatedTotalHits\": 100,\n1647\t                        \"processingTimeMs\": 5,\n1648\t                    }),\n1649\t                },\n1650\t            ],\n1651\t            offset: 0,\n1652\t            limit: 10,\n1653\t            client_requested_score: true,\n1654\t            facets: None,\n1655\t        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n1656\t        };\n1657\t\n1658\t        let result = strategy.merge(input).unwrap();\n1659\t        assert_eq!(result.hits.len(), 2);\n1660\t\n1661\t        // Small shard doc should rank first (higher score after global IDF)\n1662\t        assert_eq!(result.hits[0].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"doc-small\");\n1663\t        assert_eq!(result.hits[1].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"doc-large\");\n1664\t\n1665\t        // Scores should be preserved\n1666\t        assert_eq!(\n1667\t            result.hits[0].get(\"_rankingScore\").unwrap().as_f64(),\n1668\t     );\n1847\t    }\n1848\t\n1849\t    /// Computes Kendall tau between two rankings (document ID lists).\n1850\t    /// Used to validate merge quality against ground truth.\n1851\t    fn .keys()\n1865\t            .filter(|k| pos2.contains_key(*k))\n1866\t            .map(|k| *k)\n1867\t            .collect();\n1868\t\n1869\t        if common.len() < 2 {\n1870\t            return 0.0;\n1871\t        }\n1872\t\n1873\t        let r2_positions: Vec<usize> = common.iter().map(|id| pos2[id]).collect();\n1874\t        let (_, discordant) = count_inversions(&r2_positions);\n1875\t        let n = common.len();\n1876\t        let total = n * (n - 1) / 2;\n1877\t        let concordant = total - discordant;\n1878\t        (concordant as f64 - discordant as f64) / total as f64\n1879\t  fn simple_rng(seed: u64) -> impl FnMut() -> f64 {\n1996\t        let mut state = seed;\n1997\t        move || {\n1998\t            state = score with shard-dependent IDF skew.\n2004\t    fn fake_bm25_score(shard_id: usize, _doc_idx: usize, rng: &mut impl FnMut() -> f64) -> f64 {\n2005\t        let tf = 1.0 + rng() * 10.0;\n2006\t }\n2017\t}\n2018\t"}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"da62ac5d-d509-465b-ac28-72ebb73eea39","uuid":"e0c0daab-d20b-454f-a95e-085cbb92141f","timestamp":"2026-05-23T14:40:51.807Z","tool_use_result":{"type":"text","file":{"filePath":"/home/coding/miroir/crates/miroir-core/src/merger.rs","content":"//! Result merger: combines shard results into a single response.\n//!\n//! Supports pluggable merge strategies via the [`MergeStrategy`] trait.\n//! The default strategy is Reciprocal Rank Fusion (RRF) with k=60.\n\nuse crate::Result;\nuse serde_json::{Map, Value};\nuse std::collections::BTreeMap;\nuse std::cmp::Ordering;\n\n/// Input to the merge operation.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct MergeInput {\n    /// One response page per node in the covering set.\n    pub shard_hits: Vec<ShardHitPage>,\n\n    /// Original offset from the client request.\n    pub offset: usize,\n\n    /// Original limit from the client request.\n    pub limit: usize,\n\n    /// Whether the client requested scores in the response.\n    pub client_requested_score: bool,\n\n    /// Facet names requested (for filtering which facets to return).\n    pub facets: Option<Vec<String>>,\n\n    /// Failed shard IDs (for X-Miroir-Degraded header).\n    pub failed_shards: Vec<u32>,\n}\n\n/// Response from a single shard (node).\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct ShardHitPage {\n    /// Raw JSON response from the node.\n    pub body: Value,\n}\n\n/// Merged search result.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, serde::Serialize)]\npub struct MergedSearchResult {\n    /// Merged hits (globally sorted, offset/limit applied).\n    pub hits: Vec<Value>,\n\n    /// Aggregated facet distribution.\n    pub facet_distribution: Option<BTreeMap<String, BTreeMap<String, u64>>>,\n\n    /// Estimated total hits (sum of shard totals).\n    pub estimated_total_hits: u64,\n\n    /// Processing time in milliseconds (max across covering set).\n    pub processing_time_ms: u64,\n\n    /// Whether the response is degraded (some shards had errors).\n    pub degraded: bool,\n\n    /// Failed shard IDs (for X-Miroir-Degraded header).\n    pub failed_shards: Vec<u32>,\n}\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Merge strategy trait\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n/// Pluggable merge strategy for combining shard results.\n///\n/// Implementations define how hits from multiple shards are combined\n/// into a single globally-ranked response. The default strategy is\n/// [`RrfStrategy`] (Reciprocal Rank Fusion).\npub trait MergeStrategy: Send + Sync {\n    /// Merge search results from multiple shards into a single response.\n    fn merge(&self, input: MergeInput) -> Result<MergedSearchResult>;\n\n    /// Strategy name (for logging and `/explain` output).\n    fn name(&self) -> &'static str;\n}\n\n/// Box reference to a merge strategy (for polymorphic dispatch).\npub type DynMergeStrategy = dyn MergeStrategy;\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// RRF strategy\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n/// Default RRF constant k.\n///\n/// The value 60 is recommended in the RRF literature and used by\n/// OpenSearch for hybrid search. Smaller values amplify rank\n/// differences; larger values flatten them.\npub const DEFAULT_RRF_K: u32 = 60;\n\n/// Reciprocal Rank Fusion merge strategy.\n///\n/// Each document's contribution from a shard is `1 / (k + rank + 1)`\n/// where rank is the 0-based position. Documents appearing in\n/// multiple shards have their contributions summed. Results are\n/// sorted by total RRF score descending, with deterministic\n/// tie-breaking on primary key.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct RrfStrategy {\n    k: u32,\n}\n\nimpl RrfStrategy {\n    /// Create a new RRF strategy with the given k constant.\n    pub fn new(k: u32) -> Self {\n        Self { k: k.max(1) }\n    }\n\n    /// Create with the default k=60.\n    pub fn default_strategy() -> Self {\n        Self::new(DEFAULT_RRF_K)\n    }\n\n    /// Return the configured k value.\n    pub fn k(&self) -> u32 {\n        self.k\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Default for RrfStrategy {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self::default_strategy()\n    }\n}\n\nimpl MergeStrategy for RrfStrategy {\n    fn merge(&self, input: MergeInput) -> Result<MergedSearchResult> {\n        rrf_merge(&self.k, input)\n    }\n\n    fn name(&self) -> &'static str {\n        \"rrf\"\n    }\n}\n\n/// A document with its accumulated RRF score.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\nstruct RRFDocument {\n    /// Accumulated RRF score across all shards.\n    rrf_score: f64,\n\n    /// Primary key for tie-breaking.\n    primary_key: String,\n\n    /// The hit document (JSON object) from the highest-ranking shard.\n    hit: Map<String, Value>,\n}\n\nimpl PartialEq for RRFDocument {\n    fn eq(&self, other: &Self) -> bool {\n        self.rrf_score == other.rrf_score && self.primary_key == other.primary_key\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Eq for RRFDocument {}\n\nimpl PartialOrd for RRFDocument {\n    fn partial_cmp(&self, other: &Self) -> Option<Ordering> {\n        Some(self.cmp(other))\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Ord for RRFDocument {\n    fn cmp(&self, other: &Self) -> Ordering {\n        // Primary sort: RRF score descending (higher score = better rank)\n        match self.rrf_score.partial_cmp(&other.rrf_score) {\n            Some(Ordering::Equal) => {\n                // Secondary sort: primary key ascending for deterministic tie-breaking\n                self.primary_key.cmp(&other.primary_key)\n            }\n            Some(ord) => ord.reverse(),\n            None => {\n                // NaN case: treat as lowest score\n                if self.rrf_score.is_nan() && !other.rrf_score.is_nan() {\n                    Ordering::Less\n                } else if !self.rrf_score.is_nan() && other.rrf_score.is_nan() {\n                    Ordering::Greater\n                } else {\n                    Ordering::Equal\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Merge search results using the default RRF strategy (k=60).\n///\n/// This is a convenience wrapper around [`RrfStrategy`] for callers\n/// that don't need to customise the strategy.\npub fn merge(input: MergeInput) -> Result<MergedSearchResult> {\n    rrf_merge(&DEFAULT_RRF_K, input)\n}\n\n/// Merge search results with a specific strategy.\n///\n/// Use this when the strategy is selected from config or when you\n/// need a non-default RRF k value.\npub fn merge_with_strategy(\n    strategy: &dyn MergeStrategy,\n    input: MergeInput,\n) -> Result<MergedSearchResult> {\n    strategy.merge(input)\n}\n\n/// Core RRF merge implementation.\nfn rrf_merge(k: &u32, input: MergeInput) -> Result<MergedSearchResult> {\n    let mut estimated_total_hits = 0u64;\n    let mut max_processing_time = 0u64;\n    let mut degraded = false;\n\n    // Collect all hits with their ranks from all shards.\n    // Use a map to aggregate RRF scores for documents appearing in multiple shards.\n    let mut rrf_map: std::collections::HashMap<String, RRFDocument> = std::collections::HashMap::new();\n\n    for shard_page in &input.shard_hits {\n        let body = &shard_page.body;\n\n        // Check for degraded response.\n        if let Some(serde_json::Value::Bool(false)) = body.get(\"success\") {\n            degraded = true;\n            continue;\n        }\n\n        // Extract estimated total hits.\n        if let Some(Value::Number(n)) = body.get(\"estimatedTotalHits\") {\n            if let Some(n) = n.as_u64() {\n                estimated_total_hits = estimated_total_hits.saturating_add(n);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Extract processing time.\n        if let Some(Value::Number(n)) = body.get(\"processingTimeMs\") {\n            if let Some(n) = n.as_u64() {\n                max_processing_time = max_processing_time.max(n);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Extract hits with ranks (position in shard's results).\n        if let Some(Value::Array(hits)) = body.get(\"hits\") {\n            for (rank, hit) in hits.iter().enumerate() {\n                if let Value::Object(ref map) = hit {\n                    let map = map.clone();\n\n                    // Extract primary key for deduplication.\n                    let primary_key = map\n                        .get(\"id\")\n                        .or_else(|| map.get(\"pk\"))\n                        .and_then(|v| v.as_str())\n                        .unwrap_or(\"\")\n                        .to_string();\n\n                    // RRF contribution: 1 / (k + rank + 1)\n                    // rank is 0-based, so +1 converts to 1-based position.\n                    let rrf_contribution = 1.0 / ((*k as f64) + (rank as f64) + 1.0);\n\n                    // Aggregate RRF scores across shards.\n                    use std::collections::hash_map::Entry;\n                    match rrf_map.entry(primary_key.clone()) {\n                        Entry::Vacant(e) => {\n                            e.insert(RRFDocument {\n                                rrf_score: rrf_contribution,\n                                primary_key,\n                                hit: map,\n                            });\n                        }\n                        Entry::Occupied(mut e) => {\n                            // Document appears in multiple shards: sum RRF contributions.\n                            e.get_mut().rrf_score += rrf_contribution;\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Convert map to vec and sort by RRF score descending.\n    let mut merged_docs: Vec<_> = rrf_map.into_values().collect();\n    merged_docs.sort();\n\n    // Apply offset + limit.\n    let skip = input.offset;\n    let take = input.limit;\n    let paginated_hits: Vec<_> = merged_docs\n        .into_iter()\n        .skip(skip)\n        .take(take)\n        .collect();\n\n    // Strip reserved fields and rebuild hits.\n    let mut hits = Vec::with_capacity(paginated_hits.len());\n    for mut doc in paginated_hits {\n        // Strip _rankingScore if not requested (RRF doesn't use original scores).\n        if !input.client_requested_score {\n            doc.hit.remove(\"_rankingScore\");\n        }\n\n        // Always strip _miroir_* fields.\n        doc.hit.retain(|k, _| !k.starts_with(\"_miroir_\"));\n\n        hits.push(Value::Object(doc.hit));\n    }\n\n    // Merge facets.\n    let facet_distribution = merge_facets(&input.shard_hits, input.facets.as_deref());\n\n    Ok(MergedSearchResult {\n        hits,\n        facet_distribution,\n        estimated_total_hits,\n        processing_time_ms: max_processing_time,\n        degraded,\n        failed_shards: input.failed_shards,\n    })\n}\n\n/// Score-based merge strategy (OP#4 global-IDF).\n///\n/// This merge strategy is correct **only when** the preflight phase has\n/// provided global IDF so that scores are comparable across shards. It sorts\n/// all hits globally by `_rankingScore` descending, with deterministic\n/// tie-breaking on primary key.\n///\n/// Without global IDF, this strategy will produce incorrect rankings because\n/// shard-local scores are not comparable across shards with different document\n/// distributions.\n///\n/// Use with [`dfs_query_then_fetch_search`] in the scatter module.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy)]\npub struct ScoreMergeStrategy;\n\nimpl ScoreMergeStrategy {\n    /// Create a new score-based merge strategy.\n    pub fn new() -> Self {\n        Self\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Default for ScoreMergeStrategy {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self::new()\n    }\n}\n\nimpl MergeStrategy for ScoreMergeStrategy {\n    fn merge(&self, input: MergeInput) -> Result<MergedSearchResult> {\n        score_merge(input)\n    }\n\n    fn name(&self) -> &'static str {\n        \"score\"\n    }\n}\n\n/// Core score-based merge implementation (OP#4 global-IDF).\n///\n/// This merge strategy is correct when the preflight phase has provided\n/// global IDF so that scores are comparable across shards. It sorts all\n/// hits globally by `_rankingScore` descending, with deterministic tie-breaking\n/// on primary key.\n///\n/// Without global IDF, this strategy will produce incorrect rankings because\n/// shard-local scores are not comparable across shards with different document\n/// distributions.\nfn score_merge(input: MergeInput) -> Result<MergedSearchResult> {\n    let mut estimated_total_hits = 0u64;\n    let mut max_processing_time = 0u64;\n    let mut degraded = false;\n    let mut seen_pks = std::collections::HashSet::new();\n    let mut all_hits = Vec::new();\n\n    // Collect all hits from all shards, deduplicating by primary key.\n    // Dedup is needed because execute_scatter may push the same node response\n    // once per shard when multiple shards map to the same node.\n    for shard_page in &input.shard_hits {\n        let body = &shard_page.body;\n\n        // Check for degraded response.\n        if let Some(serde_json::Value::Bool(false)) = body.get(\"success\") {\n            degraded = true;\n            continue;\n        }\n\n        // Extract estimated total hits.\n        if let Some(Value::Number(n)) = body.get(\"estimatedTotalHits\") {\n            if let Some(n) = n.as_u64() {\n                estimated_total_hits = estimated_total_hits.saturating_add(n);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Extract processing time.\n        if let Some(Value::Number(n)) = body.get(\"processingTimeMs\") {\n            if let Some(n) = n.as_u64() {\n                max_processing_time = max_processing_time.max(n);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Extract hits.\n        if let Some(Value::Array(hits)) = body.get(\"hits\") {\n            for hit in hits {\n                if let Value::Object(map) = hit {\n                    let pk = map\n                        .get(\"id\")\n                        .or_else(|| map.get(\"pk\"))\n                        .and_then(|v| v.as_str())\n                        .unwrap_or(\"\")\n                        .to_string();\n                    if seen_pks.insert(pk) {\n                        all_hits.push(map.clone());\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Sort by score descending, then by primary key ascending for tie-breaking.\n    all_hits.sort_by(|a, b| {\n        let score_a = a.get(\"_rankingScore\")\n            .and_then(|v| v.as_f64())\n            .unwrap_or(0.0);\n        let score_b = b.get(\"_rankingScore\")\n            .and_then(|v| v.as_f64())\n            .unwrap_or(0.0);\n\n        // Extract primary keys for tie-breaking.\n        let pk_a = a.get(\"id\")\n            .or_else(|| a.get(\"pk\"))\n            .and_then(|v| v.as_str())\n            .unwrap_or(\"\");\n        let pk_b = b.get(\"id\")\n            .or_else(|| b.get(\"pk\"))\n            .and_then(|v| v.as_str())\n            .unwrap_or(\"\");\n\n        // Primary sort: score descending (higher score = better rank)\n        match score_a.partial_cmp(&score_b) {\n            Some(Ordering::Equal) => {\n                // Secondary sort: primary key ascending for deterministic tie-breaking\n                pk_a.cmp(pk_b)\n            }\n            Some(ord) => ord.reverse(),\n            None => {\n                // NaN case: treat as lowest score\n                if score_a.is_nan() && !score_b.is_nan() {\n                    Ordering::Less\n                } else if !score_a.is_nan() && score_b.is_nan() {\n                    Ordering::Greater\n                } else {\n                    Ordering::Equal\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    });\n\n    // Apply offset + limit.\n    let paginated_hits: Vec<_> = all_hits\n        .into_iter()\n        .skip(input.offset)\n        .take(input.limit)\n        .collect();\n\n    // Strip reserved fields and rebuild hits.\n    let mut hits = Vec::with_capacity(paginated_hits.len());\n    for mut hit in paginated_hits {\n        // Strip _rankingScore if not requested.\n        if !input.client_requested_score {\n            hit.remove(\"_rankingScore\");\n        }\n\n        // Always strip _miroir_* fields.\n        hit.retain(|k, _| !k.starts_with(\"_miroir_\"));\n\n        hits.push(Value::Object(hit));\n    }\n\n    // Merge facets.\n    let facet_distribution = merge_facets(&input.shard_hits, input.facets.as_deref());\n\n    Ok(MergedSearchResult {\n        hits,\n        facet_distribution,\n        estimated_total_hits,\n        processing_time_ms: max_processing_time,\n        degraded,\n        failed_shards: input.failed_shards,\n    })\n}\n\n/// Merge facet distributions from multiple shards.\n///\n/// Uses BTreeMap for stable ordering (deterministic serialization).\nfn merge_facets(\n    shard_pages: &[ShardHitPage],\n    requested_facets: Option<&[String]>,\n) -> Option<BTreeMap<String, BTreeMap<String, u64>>> {\n    let mut merged: BTreeMap<String, BTreeMap<String, u64>> = BTreeMap::new();\n\n    for shard_page in shard_pages {\n        let body = &shard_page.body;\n\n        // Meilisearch uses \"facetDistribution\" for facet results.\n        if let Some(Value::Object(facets)) = body.get(\"facetDistribution\") {\n            for (facet_name, facet_values) in facets {\n                // Skip if not requested (if a filter was provided).\n                if let Some(requested) = requested_facets {\n                    if !requested.iter().any(|f| f == facet_name) {\n                        continue;\n                    }\n                }\n\n                if let Value::Object(values_map) = facet_values {\n                    let merged_facet = merged.entry(facet_name.clone()).or_default();\n                    for (value, count) in values_map {\n                        if let Value::Number(n) = count {\n                            if let Some(n) = n.as_u64() {\n                                *merged_facet.entry(value.clone()).or_insert(0) += n;\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    if merged.is_empty() {\n        None\n    } else {\n        Some(merged)\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n    use serde_json::json;\n\n    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------\n    // Trait / strategy tests\n    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_rrf_strategy_default_matches_free_function() {\n        let input = MergeInput {\n            shard_hits: vec![make_shard_response(\n                vec![make_hit(\"doc1\", 0.9, 0), make_hit(\"doc2\", 0.7, 0)],\n                100,\n                15,\n            )],\n            offset: 0,\n            limit: 10,\n            client_requested_score: false,\n            facets: None,\n        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n        };\n\n        let strategy = RrfStrategy::default_strategy();\n        let via_trait = strategy.merge(input.clone()).unwrap();\n        let via_free = merge(input).unwrap();\n\n        assert_eq!(via_trait.hits, via_free.hits);\n        assert_eq!(via_trait.estimated_total_hits, via_free.estimated_total_hits);\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_rrf_strategy_custom_k() {\n        // With k=1, rank 0 gets 1/(1+0+1) = 0.5\n        // With k=60, rank 0 gets 1/(60+0+1) ≈ 0.0164\n        // Both should produce the same ordering for a single shard.\n        let input = MergeInput {\n            shard_hits: vec![make_shard_response(\n                vec![make_hit(\"a\", 0.9, 0), make_hit(\"b\", 0.5, 0)],\n                50,\n                10,\n            )],\n            offset: 0,\n            limit: 10,\n            client_requested_score: false,\n            facets: None,\n        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n        };\n\n        let strategy_k1 = RrfStrategy::new(1);\n        let result = strategy_k1.merge(input).unwrap();\n        assert_eq!(result.hits[0].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"a\");\n        assert_eq!(result.hits[1].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"b\");\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_merge_with_strategy_dispatches() {\n        let input = MergeInput {\n            shard_hits: vec![make_shard_response(\n                vec![make_hit(\"doc1\", 0.9, 0)],\n                50,\n                10,\n            )],\n            offset: 0,\n            limit: 10,\n            client_requested_score: false,\n            facets: None,\n        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n        };\n\n        let strategy = RrfStrategy::default_strategy();\n        let result = merge_with_strategy(&strategy, input).unwrap();\n        assert_eq!(result.hits.len(), 1);\n        assert_eq!(strategy.name(), \"rrf\");\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_rrf_strategy_k_clamped_to_one() {\n        let strategy = RrfStrategy::new(0);\n        assert_eq!(strategy.k(), 1);\n    }\n\n    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------\n    // Core merge tests\n    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    fn make_hit(id: &str, score: f64, shard: u32) -> Value {\n        json!({\n            \"id\": id,\n            \"title\": format!(\"Document {}\", id),\n            \"_rankingScore\": score,\n            \"_miroir_shard\": shard,\n        })\n    }\n\n    #[allow(dead_code)]\n    fn make_hit_ranked(id: &str, shard: u32) -> Value {\n        json!({\n            \"id\": id,\n            \"title\": format!(\"Document {}\", id),\n            \"_rankingScore\": 0.5, // RRF ignores score, only rank matters\n            \"_miroir_shard\": shard,\n        })\n    }\n\n    fn make_shard_response(\n        hits: Vec<Value>,\n        total_hits: u64,\n        processing_time: u64,\n    ) -> ShardHitPage {\n        ShardHitPage {\n            body: json!({\n                \"hits\": hits,\n                \"estimatedTotalHits\": total_hits,\n                \"processingTimeMs\": processing_time,\n                \"facetDistribution\": {},\n            }),\n        }\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_merge_basic() {\n        let input = MergeInput {\n            shard_hits: vec![make_shard_response(\n                vec![\n                    make_hit(\"doc1\", 0.9, 0),\n                    make_hit(\"doc2\", 0.7, 0),\n                ],\n                100,\n                15,\n            )],\n            offset: 0,\n            limit: 10,\n            client_requested_score: false,\n            facets: None,\n        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n        };\n\n        let result = merge(input).unwrap();\n        assert_eq!(result.hits.len(), 2);\n        assert_eq!(result.estimated_total_hits, 100);\n        assert_eq!(result.processing_time_ms, 15);\n        assert!(!result.degraded);\n\n        // Score should be stripped.\n        let hit = &result.hits[0];\n        assert!(hit.get(\"_rankingScore\").is_none());\n        assert!(hit.get(\"_miroir_shard\").is_none());\n        assert_eq!(hit.get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"doc1\");\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_merge_global_sort() {\n        let input = MergeInput {\n            shard_hits: vec![\n                make_shard_response(vec![make_hit(\"doc1\", 0.5, 0)], 50, 10),\n                make_shard_response(vec![make_hit(\"doc2\", 0.9, 1)], 50, 10),\n                make_shard_response(vec![make_hit(\"doc3\", 0.7, 2)], 50, 10),\n            ],\n            offset: 0,\n            limit: 10,\n            client_requested_score: true,\n            facets: None,\n        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n        };\n\n        let result = merge(input).unwrap();\n        assert_eq!(result.hits.len(), 3);\n\n        // RRF: all docs are at rank 0 in their respective shards.\n        // With equal ranks, tie-break by primary key (alphabetically).\n        assert_eq!(result.hits[0].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"doc1\");\n        assert_eq!(result.hits[1].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"doc2\");\n        assert_eq!(result.hits[2].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"doc3\");\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_merge_rrf_rank_ordering() {\n        // Test RRF: higher rank (lower position) contributes more to RRF score.\n        // shard0: [low_rank_doc (rank 0), mid_rank_doc (rank 10)]\n        // shard1: [high_rank_doc (rank 0)]\n        // shard2: [mid_rank_doc (rank 0) - same doc appears in two shards!]\n        //\n        // Expected RRF scores:\n        // - low_rank_doc: 1/(60+0+1) = 1/61 (only in shard0)\n        // - high_rank_doc: 1/(60+0+1) = 1/61 (only in shard1)\n        // - mid_rank_doc: 1/(60+10+1) + 1/(60+0+1) = 1/71 + 1/61 (rank 10 in shard0, rank 0 in shard2)\n        //\n        // mid_rank_doc should win because it appears in multiple shards.\n\n        let mut shard0_hits = vec![];\n        let mut shard1_hits = vec![];\n        let mut shard2_hits = vec![];\n\n        // Build shard0: low_rank_doc at position 0, mid_rank_doc at position 10\n        shard0_hits.push(make_hit(\"low_rank_doc\", 0.1, 0));\n        for i in 0..9 {\n            shard0_hits.push(make_hit(&format!(\"filler_0_{}\", i), 0.5, 0));\n        }\n        shard0_hits.push(make_hit(\"mid_rank_doc\", 0.2, 0));\n\n        // shard1: high_rank_doc at position 0\n        shard1_hits.push(make_hit(\"high_rank_doc\", 0.3, 1));\n\n        // shard2: mid_rank_doc at position 0 (same doc appears again!)\n        shard2_hits.push(make_hit(\"mid_rank_doc\", 0.4, 2));\n\n        let input = MergeInput {\n            shard_hits: vec![\n                make_shard_response(shard0_hits, 100, 10),\n                make_shard_response(shard1_hits, 100, 10),\n                make_shard_response(shard2_hits, 100, 10),\n            ],\n            offset: 0,\n            limit: 10,\n            client_requested_score: false,\n            facets: None,\n        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n        };\n\n        let result = merge(input).unwrap();\n\n        // mid_rank_doc should be first because it appears in multiple shards\n        // (RRF contributions sum: rank 10 in shard0 + rank 0 in shard2)\n        assert_eq!(result.hits[0].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"mid_rank_doc\");\n\n        // low_rank_doc and high_rank_doc both at rank 0 in their shards\n        // Tie-break by primary key alphabetically\n        assert_eq!(result.hits[1].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"high_rank_doc\");\n        assert_eq!(result.hits[2].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"low_rank_doc\");\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_merge_rrf_duplicate_handling() {\n        // Test that the same document appearing in multiple shards\n        // gets its RRF score summed.\n        //\n        // doc1 appears at rank 0 in shard0 and rank 5 in shard1\n        // doc2 appears at rank 0 in shard2\n        //\n        // RRF(doc1) = 1/(60+0+1) + 1/(60+5+1) = 1/61 + 1/66\n        // RRF(doc2) = 1/(60+0+1) = 1/61\n        //\n        // doc1 should rank higher.\n\n        let shard0_hits = vec![make_hit(\"doc1\", 0.1, 0)];\n        let mut shard1_hits = vec![];\n        let shard2_hits = vec![make_hit(\"doc2\", 0.9, 2)];\n\n        // Add filler hits to shard1 to make doc1 appear at rank 5\n        for i in 0..5 {\n            shard1_hits.push(make_hit(&format!(\"filler_1_{}\", i), 0.5, 1));\n        }\n        shard1_hits.push(make_hit(\"doc1\", 0.2, 1));\n\n        let input = MergeInput {\n            shard_hits: vec![\n                make_shard_response(shard0_hits, 50, 10),\n                make_shard_response(shard1_hits, 50, 10),\n                make_shard_response(shard2_hits, 50, 10),\n            ],\n            offset: 0,\n            limit: 10,\n            client_requested_score: false,\n            facets: None,\n        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n        };\n\n        let result = merge(input).unwrap();\n\n        // doc1 should rank higher despite lower score because\n        // it appears in multiple shards and gets RRF contribution boost\n        assert_eq!(result.hits[0].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"doc1\");\n        assert_eq!(result.hits[1].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"doc2\");\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_merge_offset_limit() {\n        let input = MergeInput {\n            shard_hits: vec![make_shard_response(\n                vec![\n                    make_hit(\"doc1\", 0.9, 0),\n                    make_hit(\"doc2\", 0.8, 0),\n                    make_hit(\"doc3\", 0.7, 0),\n                    make_hit(\"doc4\", 0.6, 0),\n                    make_hit(\"doc5\", 0.5, 0),\n                ],\n                100,\n                10,\n            )],\n            offset: 1,\n            limit: 2,\n            client_requested_score: false,\n            facets: None,\n        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n        };\n\n        let result = merge(input).unwrap();\n        assert_eq!(result.hits.len(), 2);\n        assert_eq!(result.hits[0].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"doc2\");\n        assert_eq!(result.hits[1].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"doc3\");\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_merge_preserves_score_when_requested() {\n        // RRF doesn't use scores for ranking, but we still preserve\n        // the original score field when requested.\n        let input = MergeInput {\n            shard_hits: vec![make_shard_response(\n                vec![make_hit(\"doc1\", 0.9, 0)],\n                50,\n                10,\n            )],\n            offset: 0,\n            limit: 10,\n            client_requested_score: true,\n            facets: None,\n        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n        };\n\n        let result = merge(input).unwrap();\n        assert_eq!(\n            result.hits[0].get(\"_rankingScore\").unwrap().as_f64(),\n            Some(0.9)\n        );\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_merge_rrf_ignores_scores() {\n        // Test that RRF ordering is based on rank, not score.\n        // Even though doc3 has highest score, it's ranked lower in its shard.\n        //\n        // shard0: doc2 at rank 0 with score 0.9 (same rank, tie-break by id)\n        // shard1: doc1 at rank 0 with score 0.1 (same rank, tie-break by id)\n        // shard2: doc3 at rank 2 (position 2) with score 1.0 (lower rank)\n        //\n        // RRF scores:\n        // - doc1: 1/61 (rank 0)\n        // - doc2: 1/61 (rank 0)\n        // - filler: 1/62 (rank 1)\n        // - doc3: 1/63 (rank 2)\n        //\n        // Ordering: doc1, doc2 (tie-break alphabetically), filler, then doc3\n\n        let shard0_hits = vec![make_hit(\"doc2\", 0.9, 0)]; // High score, rank 0\n        let shard1_hits = vec![make_hit(\"doc1\", 0.1, 0)]; // Low score, rank 0\n        let shard2_hits = vec![\n            make_hit(\"filler\", 0.5, 2),\n            make_hit(\"filler2\", 0.5, 2),\n            make_hit(\"doc3\", 1.0, 2),  // Highest score, but rank 2\n        ];\n\n        let input = MergeInput {\n            shard_hits: vec![\n                make_shard_response(shard0_hits, 50, 10),\n                make_shard_response(shard1_hits, 50, 10),\n                make_shard_response(shard2_hits, 50, 10),\n            ],\n            offset: 0,\n            limit: 10,\n            client_requested_score: true,\n            facets: None,\n        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n        };\n\n        let result = merge(input).unwrap();\n\n        // doc1 and doc2 both at rank 0, tie-break alphabetically\n        assert_eq!(result.hits[0].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"doc1\");\n        assert_eq!(result.hits[1].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"doc2\");\n        // filler and filler2 at rank 1\n        assert_eq!(result.hits[2].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"filler\");\n        assert_eq!(result.hits[3].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"filler2\");\n        // doc3 at rank 2, comes last despite highest score\n        assert_eq!(result.hits[4].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"doc3\");\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_merge_strips_miroir_fields() {\n        let input = MergeInput {\n            shard_hits: vec![make_shard_response(\n                vec![json!({\n                    \"id\": \"doc1\",\n                    \"title\": \"Test\",\n                    \"_rankingScore\": 0.9,\n            offset: 0,\n            limit: 10,\n            client_requested_score: false,\n            facets: None,\n        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n        };\n\n        let result = merge(input).unwrap();\n        let hit = &result.hits[0];\n\n        assert!(hit.get(\"_rankingScore\").is_none());\n        assert!(hit.get(\"_miroir_shard\").is_none());\n        assert!(hit.get(\"_miroir_node\").is_none());\n        assert!(hit.get(\"_miroir_group\").is_none());\n\n        // Non-reserved fields preserved.\n        assert_eq!(hit.get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"doc1\");\n        assert_eq!(hit.get(\"title\").unwrap(), \"Test\");\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_merge_facets() {\n        let shard1 = ShardHitPage {\n            body: json!({\n                \"hits\": [],\n                \"estimatedTotalHits\": 100,\n                \"processingTimeMs\": 10,\n                \"facetDistribution\": {\n                    \"category\": {\n                        \"electronics\": 50,\n                        \"books\": 30,\n                    },\n                    \"brand\": {\n                        \"apple\": 20,\n                    },\n                },\n            }),\n        };\n\n        let shard2 = ShardHitPage {\n            body: json!({\n                \"hits\": [],\n                \"estimatedTotalHits\": 100,\n                \"processingTimeMs\": 15,\n                \"facetDistribution\": {\n                    \"category\": {\n                        \"electronics\": 40,\n                        \"clothing\": 25,\n                    },\n                    \"brand\": {\n                        \"samsung\": 15,\n                    },\n                },\n            }),\n        };\n\n        let input = MergeInput {\n            shard_hits: vec![shard1, shard2],\n            offset: 0,\n            limit: 10,\n            client_requested_score: false,\n            facets: None,\n        failed_shards:  assert_eq!(brand.get(\"samsung\"), Some(&15));\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_merge_facets_filter() {\n        let shard = ShardHitPage {\n            body: json!({\n                \"hits\":       make_shard_response(vec![make_hit(\"apple\", 0.5, 1)], 50, 10),\n            ],\n            offset: 0,\n            limit: 10,\n            client_requested_score: false,\n            facets: {\n            all_hits.push(make_hit(&format!(\"doc{:02}\", i), (50 - i) as f64 / 100.0, 0));\n        }\n\n        let input = MergeInput {\n            shard_hits: vec![make_shard_response(all_hits, 50, 10)],\n            offset: 0,\n            limit: 50,\n            client_requested_score: false,\n            facets: None,\n        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n        };\n\n        let full_result = merge(input.clone()).unwrap();\n        assert_eq!(full_result.hits.len(), 50);\n\n        // Now fetch in pages of 10 and verify they match.\n        for page in 0..5 {\n            let page_input = MergeInput {\n                shard_hits: input.shard_hits.clone(),\n                offset: page * 10,\n                limit: 10,\n                client_requested_score: false,\n                facets: None,\n        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n            };\n            let page_result = merge(page_input).unwrap();\n\n            let start =         page\n            );\n        }\n    }\n\n    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------\n    // RRF correctness properties\n    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_rrf_cross_shard_replication_boost() {\n        // Key RRF property: a document appearing in multiple shards\n        // gets a higher merged score than a single-shard document,\n        // even if it ranks lower within each shard.\n        //\n        // doc-replicated: rank 5 in shard0, rank 5 in shard1\n        //   RRF = 1/(60+5+1) + 1/(60+5+1) = 2/66 ≈ 0.0303\n        // doc-single: rank 0 in shard2\n        //   RRF = 1/(60+0+1) = 1/61 ≈ 0.0164\n        //\n        // doc-replicated should rank higher.\n\n        let mut shard0 = vec![];\n        let mut shard1 = vec![];\n        for i in 0..5 {\n            shard0.push(make_hit(&format!(\"filler0-{}\", i), 0.5, 0));\n            shard1.push(make_hit(&format!(\"filler1-{}\", i), 0.5, 1));\n        }\n        shard0.push(make_hit(\"doc-replicated\", 0.1, 0));\n        shard1.push(make_hit(\"doc-replicated\", 0.1, 1));\n\n        let shard2 = vec![make_hit(\"doc-single\", 0.99, 2)];\n\n        let strategy = RrfStrategy::default_strategy();\n        let result = strategy\n            .merge(MergeInput {\n                shard_hits: vec![\n                    make_shard_response(shard0, 100, 10),\n                    make_shard_response(shard1, 100, 10),\n                    make_shard_response(shard2, 100, 10),\n                ],\n                offset: 0,\n                limit: 20,\n                client_requested_score: false,\n                facets: None,\n        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n            })\n            .unwrap();\n\n        let ids: Vec<_> = result.hits.iter().filter_map(|h| h.get(\"id\").and_then(|v| v.as_str())).collect();\n        let rep_pos = ids.iter().position(|&id| id == \"doc-replicated\").unwrap();\n        let single_pos = ids.iter().position(|&id| id == \"doc-single\").unwrap();\n        assert!(\n            rep_pos < single_pos,\n            \"Replicated doc at pos {} should rank above single doc at pos {}\",\n            rep_pos,\n            single_pos\n        );\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_rrf_immune_to_score_scale() {\n        // RRF uses rank only: scores of 0.001 vs 0.999 don't affect ordering.\n        // Two shards with wildly different score ranges should produce the\n        // same merge as two shards with uniform scores.\n        let shard_a = ShardHitPage {\n            body: json!({\n                \"hits\": [\n                    {\"id\": \"a1\", \"_rankingScore\": 0.001},\n                    {\"id\": \"a2\", \"_rankingScore\": 0.002},\n                ],\n                \"estimatedTotalHits\": 2,\n                \"processingTimeMs\": 5,\n            }),\n        };\n        let shard_b = ShardHitPage {\n            body: json!({\n                \"hits\": [\n                    {\"id\": \"b1\", \"_rankingScore\": 0.999},\n                    {\"id\": \"b2\", \"_rankingScore\": 0.998},\n                ],\n                \"estimatedTotalHits\": 2,\n                \"processingTimeMs\": 5,\n            }),\n        };\n\n        let strategy = RrfStrategy::default_strategy();\n        let result = strategy\n            .merge(MergeInput {\n                shard_hits: vec![shard_a, shard_b],\n                offset: 0,\n                limit: 10,\n                client_requested_score: false,\n                facets: None,\n        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n            })\n            .unwrap();\n\n        // All at rank 0 or 1 — tie-break alphabetically within each rank tier.\n        // rank 0: a1, b1 → sort by id → a1, b1\n        // rank 1: a2, b2 → sort by id → a2, b2\n        let ids: Vec<_> = result.hits.iter().filter_map(|h| h.get(\"id\").and_then(|v| v.as_str())).collect();\n        assert_eq!(ids, vec![\"a1\", \"b1\", \"a2\", \"b2\"]);\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_rrf_deterministic_with_same_input() {\n        // RRF merge is a pure \"doc1\".into(),\n            hit: Map::new(),\n        };\n        let b = super::RRFDocument {\n            rrf_score: 1.0,\n            primary_key: \"doc1\".into(),\n            hit: Map::new(),\n        };\n        assert_eq!(a, b);\n\n        let c = super::RRFDocument {\n            rrf_score: 1.0,\n            primary_key: \"doc2\".into(),\n            hit: Map::new(),\n        };\n        assert_ne!(a, c);\n\n        // NaN: both NaN → Equal\n        let nan_a = super::RRFDocument {\n            rrf_score: f64::NAN,\n            primary_key: \"x\".into(),\n            hit: Map::new(),\n        };\n        let nan_b = super::RRFDocument {\n            rrf_score: f64::NAN,\n            primary_key: \"x\".into(),\n            hit: Map::new(),\n        };\n        assert_eq!(nan_a.cmp(&nan_b), Ordering::Equal);\n\n        // NaN vs real: NaN is Less\n        let real = super::RRFDocument {\n            rrf_score: 1.0,\n            primary_key: \"x\".into(),\n            hit: Map::new(),\n        };\n        assert_eq!(nan_a.cmp(&real), Ordering::Less);\n        assert_eq!(real.cmp(&nan_a), Ordering::Greater);\n    }\n\n    //         50,\n                    10,\n                ),\n                // Shard 1: high scores (these should rank higher)\n                make_shard_response(\n                    vec![\n                        make_hit(\"doc-high-1\", 0.9, 1),\n                        make_hit(\"doc-high-2\", 0.8, 1),\n                    ],\n                    50,\n                    10,\n                ),\n            ],\n            offset: 0,\n            limit: 10,\n            client_requested_score: true,\n            facets: None,\n        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n        };\n\n        let
