  ///\n    /// This simulates the scenario described in P12.OP4:\n    /// - Shard 0 has 1000 docs, term \"rust\" appears in 100 (df=100)\n    /// - Shard 1 has 100 docs, term \"rust\" appears in 50 (df=50)\n    ///\n    /// Without global IDF:\n    /// - Local IDF(shard 0) = log((1000-100+0.5)/(100+0.5)+1) ≈ 2.2\n    /// - Local IDF(shard 1) = log((100-50+0.5)/(50+0.5)+1) ≈ 0.7\n    ///\n    /// With global IDF:\n    /// - Global N = 1100, global df = 150\n    /// - Global IDF = log((1100-150+0.5)/(150+0.5)+1) ≈ 1.8\n    ///\n    /// A document with tf=3 for \"rust\" in each shard:\n    /// - Shard 0 score (local IDF): ~3 * 2.2 = 6.6\n    /// - Shard 1 score (local IDF): ~3 * 0.7 = 2.1\n    ///\n    /// Without global IDF, shard 0 doc ranks higher despite shard 1 having\n    /// much higher term density (50/100 vs 100/1000).\n    ///\n    /// With global IDF, both shards use IDF=1.8, and the doc with higher\n    /// term density (normalized by document length) ranks correctly.\n    #[test]\n    fn test_score_merge_skewed_corpus_integration() {\n        // Simulate global IDF applied (scores are now comparable)\n        let strategy = ScoreMergeStrategy::new();\n\n        // Doc in large shard with high term frequency but low density\n        let doc_large_shard = json!({\n            \"id\": \"doc-large\",\n            \"title\": \"Rust in Large Shard\",\n            \"_rankingScore\": 0.75, // After global-IDF normalization\n        });\n\n        // Doc in small shard with lower term frequency but high density\n        let doc_small_shard = json!({\n            \"id\": \"doc-small\",\n            \"title\": \"Rust in Small Shard\",\n            \"_rankingScore\": 0.85, // After global-IDF normalization\n        });\n\n        // With global IDF, the small shard doc should rank higher\n        // because its term density is higher (50/100 vs 100/1000)\n        let input = MergeInput {\n            shard_hits: vec![\n                ShardHitPage {\n                    body: json!({\n                        \"hits\": [doc_large_shard],\n                        \"estimatedTotalHits\": 1000,\n                        \"processingTimeMs\": 10,\n                    }),\n                },\n                ShardHitPage {\n                    body: json!({\n                        \"hits\": [doc_small_shard],\n                        \"estimatedTotalHits\": 100,\n                        \"processingTimeMs\": 5,\n                    }),\n                },\n            ],\n            offset: 0,\n            limit: 10,\n            client_requested_score: true,\n            facets: None,\n        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n        };\n\n        let result = strategy.merge(input).unwrap();\n        assert_eq!(result.hits.len(), 2);\n\n        // Small shard doc should rank first (higher score after global IDF)\n        assert_eq!(result.hits[0].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"doc-small\");\n        assert_eq!(result.hits[1].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"doc-large\");\n\n        // Scores should be preserved\n        assert_eq!(\n            result.hits[0].get(\"_rankingScore\").unwrap().as_f64(),\n            Some(0.85)\n        );\n        assert_eq!(\n            result.hits[1].get(\"_rankingScore\").unwrap().as_f64(),\n            Some(0.75)\n        );\n    }\n\n    /// Test that demonstrates the failure mode without global IDF.\n    ///\n    /// This shows what happens when scores are NOT comparable across shards:\n    /// score-based merge produces incorrect rankings, while RRF at least\n    /// produces consistent (though not optimal) results.\n    #[test]\n    fn test_score_merge_without_global_idf_fails() {\n        // Simulate the bug: shard-local IDF produces incomparable scores\n        let strategy = ScoreMergeStrategy::new();\n\n        // Shard 0: large shard, inflated local IDF (shard has term rarity)\n        let doc_shard0 = json!({\n            \"id\": \"doc-inflated\",\n            \"title\": \"Document in Large Shard\",\n            \"_rankingScore\": 0.95, // Inflated due to high local IDF\n        });\n\n        // Shard 1: small shard, deflated local IDF (term is common here)\n        let doc_shard1 = json!({\n            \"id\": \"doc-deflated\",\n            \"title\": \"Document in Small Shard\",\n            \"_rankingScore\": 0.60, // Deflated due to low local IDF\n        });\n\n        let input = MergeInput {\n            shard_hits: vec![\n                ShardHitPage {\n                    body: json!({\n                        \"hits\": [doc_shard0],\n                        \"estimatedTotalHits\": 10000,\n                        \"processingTimeMs\": 15,\n                    }),\n                },\n                ShardHitPage {\n                    body: json!({\n                        \"hits\": [doc_shard1],\n                        \"estimatedTotalHits\": 100,\n                        \"processingTimeMs\": 5,\n                    }),\n                },\n            ],\n            offset: 0,\n            limit: 10,\n            client_requested_score: true,\n            facets: None,\n        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n        };\n\n        let result = strategy.merge(input).unwrap();\n\n        // Without global IDF, score-based merge trusts the inflated scores\n        assert_eq!(result.hits[0].get(\"id\").unwrap(), \"doc-inflated\");\n\n        // This is WRONG: doc-deflated has much higher term density but\n        // ranks lower due to shard-local IDF skew.\n        //\n        // The solution is the preflight phase (dfs_query_then_fetch_search)\n        // which computes global IDF so scores are comparable.\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_score_merge_default_impl() {\n        let via_default: ScoreMergeStrategy = Default::default();\n        let via_constructor = ScoreMergeStrategy::new();\n        assert_eq!(via_default.name(), via_constructor.name());\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_score_merge_empty_input() {\n        let strategy = ScoreMergeStrategy::new();\n        let input = MergeInput {\n            shard_hits: vec![],\n            offset: 0,\n            limit: 10,\n            client_requested_score: false,\n            facets: None,\n        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n        };\n\n        let result = strategy.merge(input).unwrap();\n        assert_eq!(result.hits.len(), 0);\n        assert_eq!(result.estimated_total_hits, 0);\n    }\n\n    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------\n    // P12.OP4 RRF skew validation\n    // -----------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    /// Validates the P12.OP4 finding: RRF merge with extreme shard skew\n    /// produces incorrect global rankings because it gives equal weight\n    /// to all shards regardless of their size.\n    ///\n    /// Scenario: 10 shards where shard 0 has 93K docs (93%) and shard 9\n    /// has 10 docs (0.01%). RRF assigns identical scores to rank-0 hits\n    /// from all shards, so a mediocre hit from the tiny shard ranks\n    /// equally with the best hit from the dominant shard.\n    ///\n    /// Benchmark result (10K queries, skewed corpus):\n    ///   Score merge:   τ = 0.79  (95% CI [0.787, 0.801]) — FAIL\n    ///   RRF merge:     τ = 0.14  (95% CI [0.134, 0.140]) — FAIL\n    ///   DFS preflight: τ = 0.98  (95% CI [0.982, 0.982]) — PASS\n    ///\n    /// Conclusion: RRF alone does NOT solve cross-shard comparability.\n    /// Global-IDF preflight (dfs_query_then_fetch) is required.\n    #[test]\n    fn test_rrf_skewed_shards_equal_weight_problem() {\n        // Shard 0 (dominant): doc-best should be the global #1 result.\n        // It has the highest score and appears in the shard with 93% of docs.\n        let shard_dominant = make_shard_response(\n            vec![\n                make_hit(\"doc-best\", 0.95, 0),      // True global #1\n                make_hit(\"doc-good\", 0.90, 0),       // True global #2\n                make_hit(\"doc-ok\", 0.85, 0),         // True global #3\n                make_hit(\"doc-mediocre\", 0.70, 0),   // True global #4\n                make_hit(\"doc-weak\", 0.60, 0),       // True global #5\n            ],\n            93_000,\n            10,\n        );\n\n        // Shard 9 (tiny, 10 docs): due to local IDF skew, irrelevant docs\n        // can appear at rank 0 with inflated local scores.\n        let shard_tiny = make_shard_response(\n            vec![\n                make_hit(\"doc-irrelevant\", 0.98, 9), // Inflated local IDF → high score\n                make_hit(\"doc-noise\", 0.92, 9),\n            ],\n            10,\n            2,\n        );\n\n        let strategy = RrfStrategy::default_strategy();\n        let result = strategy\n            .merge(MergeInput {\n                shard_hits: vec![shard_dominant, shard_tiny],\n                offset: 0,\n                limit: 10,\n                client_requested_score: true,\n                facets: None,\n        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n            })\n            .unwrap();\n\n        let ids: Vec<_> = result\n            .hits\n            .iter()\n            .filter_map(|h| h.get(\"id\").and_then(|v| v.as_str()))\n            .collect();\n\n        // RRF gives equal rank weight to both shards.\n        // Rank 0 from dominant shard: 1/61 ≈ 0.0164\n        // Rank 0 from tiny shard:     1/61 ≈ 0.0164 (identical!)\n        //\n        // Tie-breaking falls to primary key (alphabetical), NOT relevance.\n        // doc-best and doc-irrelevant both get RRF score 1/61.\n        // Alphabetically: doc-best < doc-irrelevant → doc-best wins the tie.\n        //\n        // But doc-irrelevant still ranks above doc-good, doc-ok, doc-mediocre,\n        // and doc-weak — all of which are more relevant globally.\n        assert_eq!(ids[0], \"doc-best\");      // Tie-break win (alphabetical)\n        assert_eq!(ids[1], \"doc-irrelevant\"); // Tie-break loss, but still rank 2!\n\n        // doc-irrelevant (globally irrelevant) ranks ABOVE doc-good (global #2)\n        let irrelevant_pos = ids.iter().position(|&id| id == \"doc-irrelevant\").unwrap();\n        let good_pos = ids.iter().position(|&id| id == \"doc-good\").unwrap();\n        assert!(\n            irrelevant_pos < good_pos,\n            \"RRF skew bug: irrelevant doc (pos {}) ranks above doc-good (pos {})\",\n            irrelevant_pos,\n            good_pos,\n        );\n    }\n\n    /// Computes Kendall tau between two rankings (document ID lists).\n    /// Used to validate merge quality against ground truth.\n    fn kendall_tau(ranking1: &[String], ranking2: &[String]) -> f64 {\n        let pos1: std::collections::HashMap<&str, usize> = ranking1\n            .iter()\n            .enumerate()\n            .map(|(i, id)| (id.as_str(), i))\n            .collect();\n        let pos2: std::collections::HashMap<&str, usize> = ranking2\n            .iter()\n            .enumerate()\n            .map(|(i, id)| (id.as_str(), i))\n            .collect();\n\n        let common: Vec<&str> = pos1\n            .keys()\n            .filter(|k| pos2.contains_key(*k))\n            .map(|k| *k)\n            .collect();\n\n        if common.len() < 2 {\n            return 0.0;\n        }\n\n        let r2_positions: Vec<usize> = common.iter().map(|id| pos2[id]).collect();\n        let (_, discordant) = count_inversions(&r2_positions);\n        let n = common.len();\n        let total = n * (n - 1) / 2;\n        let concordant = total - discordant;\n        (concordant as f64 - discordant as f64) / total as f64\n    }\n\n    fn count_inversions(arr: &[usize]) -> (Vec<usize>, usize) {\n        if arr.len() <= 1 {\n            return (arr.to_vec(), 0);\n        }\n        let mid = arr.len() / 2;\n        let (left, inv_l) = count_inversions(&arr[..mid]);\n        let (right, inv_r) = count_inversions(&arr[mid..]);\n\n        let mut merged = Vec::with_capacity(arr.len());\n        let mut inv = inv_l + inv_r;\n        let (mut i, mut j) = (0, 0);\n\n        while i < left.len() && j < right.len() {\n            if left[i] <= right[j] {\n                merged.push(left[i]);\n                i += 1;\n            } else {\n                merged.push(right[j]);\n                inv += left.len() - i;\n                j += 1;\n            }\n        }\n        merged.extend_from_slice(&left[i..]);\n        merged.extend_from_slice(&right[j..]);\n        (merged, inv)\n    }\n\n    /// End-to-end validation: RRF merge on skewed shards produces τ < 0.95\n    /// against ground truth (single-index ranking).\n    ///\n    /// This is a scaled-down version of the 10K-query Python benchmark.\n    #[test]\n    fn test_rrf_skewed_shards_tau_below_threshold() {\n        let k = DEFAULT_RRF_K;\n\n        // Build 5 shards with skewed sizes: [100, 500, 2000, 5000, 10000]\n        // Ground truth: all 17600 docs in one index, sorted by score.\n        let mut all_docs: Vec<(String, f64)> = Vec::new();\n        let mut shard_docs: Vec<Vec<(String, f64)>> = vec![vec![], vec![], vec![], vec![], vec![]];\n        let shard_sizes = [100, 500, 2000, 5000, 10000];\n\n        let mut rng = simple_rng(42);\n        for (shard_id, &size) in shard_sizes.iter().enumerate() {\n            for i in 0..size {\n                // Deterministic pseudo-random scores\n                let score = fake_bm25_score(shard_id, i, &mut rng);\n                let doc_id = format!(\"s{}-d{:06}\", shard_id, i);\n                all_docs.push((doc_id.clone(), score));\n                shard_docs[shard_id].push((doc_id, score));\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Ground truth: global sort by score descending\n        all_docs.sort_by(|a, b| b.1.partial_cmp(&a.1).unwrap_or(std::cmp::Ordering::Equal));\n        let ground_truth: Vec<String> = all_docs.iter().take(100).map(|(id, _)| id.clone()).collect();\n\n        // Per-shard: sort locally (simulates local BM25 with local IDF)\n        for docs in &mut shard_docs {\n            docs.sort_by(|a, b| b.1.partial_cmp(&a.1).unwrap_or(std::cmp::Ordering::Equal));\n        }\n\n        // RRF merge using the actual Rust merger\n        let shard_pages: Vec<ShardHitPage> = shard_docs\n            .iter()\n            .map(|docs| {\n                let hits: Vec<Value> = docs\n                    .iter()\n                    .take(200)\n                    .map(|(id, score)| {\n                        json!({\n                            \"id\": id,\n                            \"_rankingScore\": score,\n                        })\n                    })\n                    .collect();\n                ShardHitPage {\n                    body: json!({\n                        \"hits\": hits,\n                        \"estimatedTotalHits\": docs.len(),\n                        \"processingTimeMs\": 10,\n                    }),\n                }\n            })\n            .collect();\n\n        let strategy = RrfStrategy::new(k);\n        let result = strategy\n            .merge(MergeInput {\n                shard_hits: shard_pages,\n                offset: 0,\n                limit: 100,\n                client_requested_score: true,\n                facets: None,\n        failed_shards: Vec::new(),\n            })\n            .unwrap();\n\n        let rrf_ranking: Vec<String> = result\n            .hits\n            .iter()\n            .filter_map(|h| h.get(\"id\").and_then(|v| v.as_str()).map(String::from))\n            .collect();\n\n        let tau = kendall_tau(&ground_truth, &rrf_ranking);\n\n        // RRF with skewed shards should produce τ well below 0.95.\n        assert!(\n            tau < 0.95,\n            \"RRF tau = {:.4}, expected < 0.95 with skewed shards\",\n            tau,\n        );\n    }\n\n    /// Simple deterministic PRNG for reproducible test scores.\n    fn simple_rng(seed: u64) -> impl FnMut() -> f64 {\n        let mut state = seed;\n        move || {\n            state = state.wrapping_mul(6_364_136_223_846_793_005).wrapping_add(1);\n            (state >> 33) as f64 / (1u64 << 31) as f64\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Simulates a BM25-like score with shard-dependent IDF skew.\n    fn fake_bm25_score(shard_id: usize, _doc_idx: usize, rng: &mut impl FnMut() -> f64) -> f64 {\n        let tf = 1.0 + rng() * 10.0;\n        // Larger shards have lower IDF for common terms (simulating skew)\n        let shard_weight = match shard_id {\n            0 => 0.3,\n            1 => 0.5,\n            2 => 0.7,\n            3 => 0.9,\n            4 => 1.0,\n            _ => 0.5,\n        };\n        tf * shard_weight + rng() * 0.5\n    }\n}\n","numLines":2018,"startLine":1,"totalLines":2018}}}

serde_json::json!(self.offset + self.limit);\n354\t\n355\t        // Set offset to 0 on individual nodes (coordinator handles offset)\n356\t        body[\"offset\"] = serde_json::json!(0);\n357\t\n358\t        // Ensure query is set\n359\t        if let Some(q) = &self.query {\n360\t            body[\"q\"] = serde_json::json!(q);\n361\t        }\n362\t\n363\t        // Ensure filter is set if provided\n364\t        if let Some(filter) = &self.filter {\n365\t            body[\"filter\"] = filter.clone();\n366\t        }\n367\t\n368\t        // Ensure facets are set if provided\n369\t        if let Some(facets) = &self.facets {\n370\t            body[\"facets\"] = serde_json::json!(facets);\n371\t        }\n372\t\n373\t        body\n374\t    }\n375\t}\n376\t\n377\t#[derive(Debug)]\n378\tpub struct ScatterResult {\n379\t    pub shard_pages: Vec<ShardHitPage>,\n380\t    pub failed_shards: HashMap<u32, NodeError>,\n381\t    pub partial: bool,\n382\t    pub deadline_exceeded: bool,\n383\t}\n384\t\n385\t#[instrument(skip_all, fields(query_seq, rf, shard_count))]\n386\tpub fn plan_search_scatter(\n387\t    topology: &Topology,\n388\t    query_seq: u64,\n389\t    rf: usize,\n390\t    shard_count: u32,\n391\t) -> ScatterPlan {\n392\t    let chosen_group = query_group(query_seq, topology.replica_group_count());\n393\t\n394\t    let selected);\n411\t    }\n412\t\n413\t    ScatterPlan {\n414\t        chosen_group,\n415\t        target_shards: (0..shard_count).collect(),\n416\t        shard_to_node,\n417\t        deadline_ms: 5000,\n418\t        hedging_eligible: group.node_count() > 1,\n419\t    }\n420\t}\n421\t\n422\t/// Plan search scatter with settings version floor filtering (plan §13.5).\n423\t///\n424\t/// Excludes nodes whose settings version for the given index is below `floor`.\n425\t/// Returns None if no covering set can be assembled (caller should return 503).\n426\tpub fn plan_search_scatter_with_version_floor(\n427\t    topology: &Topology,\n428\t    query_seq: u64,\n429\t    rf: usize,\n430\t    shard_count: u32,\n431\t    index: &str,\n432\t    floor: u64,\n433\t    version_checker: &impl Fn(&str, &str) -> u64,\n434\t) -> Option<ScatterPlan> {\n435\t    let chosen_group = query_group(query_seq, topology.replica_group_count());\n436\t\n437\t    let group = topology.group(chosen_group)?;\n438\t\n439\t    let covering = covering_set_with_version_floor(\n440\t        shard_count,\n441\t        group,\n442\t        rf,\n443\t        query_seq,\n444\t        index,\n445\t        floor,\n446\t        version_checker,\n447\t    )?;\n448\t\n449\t    let mut shard_to_node = HashMap::new();\n450\t    for shard_id in 0..shard_count {\n451\t        let replicas .iter()\n455\t            .filter(|node_id| {\n456\t                let version = version_checker(index, node_id.as_str());\n457\t                version >= floor\n458\t            })\n459\t            .collect();\n460\t\n461\t        if eligible.is_empty() {\n462\t            return None;\n463\t        }\n464\t\n465\t        let selected = eligible[query_seq as usize % eligible.len()];\n466\t        shard_to_node.insert(shard_id, selected.clone());\n467\t    }\n468\t\n469\t    Some(ScatterPlan {\n470\t        chosen_group,\n471\t        target_shards: (0..shard_count).collect(),\n472\t        shard_to_node,\n473\t        deadline_ms: 5000,\n474\t        hedging_eligible: group.node_count() > 1,\n475\t    })\n476\t}\n477\t\n478\t/// Plan search scatter for a specific replica group (plan §13.6 session pinning).\n479\t///\n480\t/// Used when a session has a pending write and needs to read from the pinned group\n481\t/// to ensure read-your-writes consistency.\n482\tpub fn plan_search_scatter_for_group(\n483\t    topology: &Topology,\n484\t    query_seq: u64,\n485\t    rf: usize,\n486\t    shard_count: u32,\n487\t    pinned_group: u32,\n488\t) -> Option<ScatterPlan> {\n489\t    let group = topology.group(pinned_group)?;\n490\t\n491\t    let mut shard_to_node = HashMap::new();\n492\t    for shard_id in 0..shard_count {\n493\t        let replicas = crate::router::assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, group.nodes(), rf);\n494\t        if replicas.is_empty() {\n495\t            continue;\n496\t        }\n497\t        let selected = replicas[query_seq as usize % replicas.len()].clone();\n498\t        shard_to_node.insert(shard_id, selected);\n499\t    }\n500\t\n501\t    Some(ScatterPlan {\n502\t        chosen_group: pinned_group,\n503\t        target_shards: (0..shard_count).collect(),\n504\t        shard_to_node,\n505\t        deadline_ms: 5000,\n506\t        hedging_eligible: group.node_count() > 1,\n507\t    })\n508\t}\n509\t\n510\t#[instrument(skip_all, fields(node_count))]\n511\tpub async fn execute_scatter<C: NodeClient>(\n512\t    plan: ScatterPlan,\n513\t    client: &C,\n514\t    req: SearchRequest,\n515\t    topology: &Topology,\n516\t    policy: UnavailableShardPolicy,\n517\t) -> Result<ScatterResult> {\n518\t    let mut node_to_shards: HashMap<NodeId, Vec<u32>> = HashMap::new();\n519\t    for (&shard_id, node_id) in &plan.shard_to_node {\n520\t        if plan.target_shards.contains(&shard_id) {\n521\t            node_to_shards.entry(node_id.clone()).or_default().push(shard_id);\n522\t        }\n523\t    }\n524\t    tracing::Span::current().record(\"node_count\", node_to_shards.len());\n525\t\n526\t    let mut shard_pages = Vec::new();\n527\t    let mut failed_shards = HashMap::new();\n528\t    let mut deadline_exceeded = false;\n529\t\n530\t    let mut tasks = Vec::new();\n531\t    for (node_id, shards) in node_to_shards {\n532\t        let node = match topology.node(&node_id) {\n533\t            Some(n) => n.clone(),\n534\t            None => {\n535\t                for shard_id in shards {\n536\t                    failed_shards.insert(shard_id, NodeError::NetworkError(\"node not in topology\".to_string()));\n537\t                }\n538\t                continue;\n539\t            }\n540\t        };\n541\t        let client_ref = client;\n542\t        let req_clone = req.clone();\n543\t        let node_id_clone = node_id.clone();\n544\t        let shard_count = shards.len();\n545\t        // Create a span for this node's scatter call\n546\t        let span = info_span!(\n547\t            \"scatter_node\",\n548\t            node_id = %node_id_clone,\n549\t            address = %node.address,\n550\t            shard_count = shard_count,\n551\t        );\n552\t        tasks.push(async move {\n553\t            let result = client_ref.search_node(&node_id_clone, &node.address, &req_clone).await;\n554\t            (node_id_clone, shards, result)\n555\t        }.instrument(span));\n556\t    }\n557\t\n558\t    let results = futures_util::future::join_all(tasks).await;\n559\t\n560\t    for (_node_id, shards, result) in results {\n561\t        match result {\n562\t            Ok(body) => {\n563\t                for _shard_id in shards {\n564\t                    shard_pages.push(ShardHitPage { body: body.clone() });\n565\t                }\n566\t            }\n567\t            Err(NodeError::Timeout) => {\n568\t                deadline_exceeded = true;\n569\t                for shard_id in shards { failed_shards.insert(shard_id, NodeError::Timeout); }\n570\t            }\n571\t            Err(e) => {\n572\t                for shard_id in shards { failed_shards.insert(shard_id, e.clone()); }\n573\t            }\n574\t        }\n575\t    }\n576\t\n577\t    let partial = !failed_shards.is_empty();\n578\t\n579\t    match policy {\n580\t        UnavailableShardPolicy::Error => {\n581\t            if !failed_shards.is_empty() {\n582\t                return Err(crate::error::MiroirError::Routing(format!(\"{} shard(s) unavailable\", failed_shards.len())));\n583\t            }\n584\t        }\n585\t        UnavailableShardPolicy::Partial => {}\n586\t        UnavailableShardPolicy::Fallback => {\n587\t            // Group-unavailability fallback: try other replica groups for failed shards\n588\t            if !failed_shards.is_empty() {\n589\t                let mut fallback_pages = Vec::new();\n590\t                let mut remaining_failed = HashMap::new();\n591\t\n592\t                for (&shard_id, error) in &failed_shards {\n593\t                    let mut fallback_succeeded = false;\n594\t\n595\t                    // Try each other replica group\n596\t                    for group_id in 0..topology.replica_group_count() {\n597\t                        if group_id == plan.chosen_group {\n598\t                            continue; // Skip the already-tried group\n599\t                        }\n600\t\n601\t                        if let Some(group) = topology.group(group_id) {\n602\t                            let replicas = crate::router::assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, group.nodes(), topology.rf());\n603\t                            if replicas.is_empty() {\n604\t                                continue;\n605\t                            }\n606\t\n607\t                            // Try each replica in the fallback group\n608\t                            for node_id in replicas {\n609\t                                if let Some(node) = topology.node(&node_id) {\n610\t                                    match client.search_node(&node_id, &node.address, &req).await {\n611\t                                        Ok(body) => {\n612\t                                            fallback_pages.push(ShardHitPage { body });\n613\t                                            fallback_succeeded = true;\n614\t                                            break;\n615\t                                        }\n616\t                                        Err(_) => {\n617\t                                            continue; // Try next replica\n618\t                                        }\n619\t                                    }\n620\t                                }\n621\t                            }\n622\t\n623\t                            if fallback_succeeded {\n624\t                                break; // Found a working replica\n625\t                            }\n626\t                        }\n627\t                    }\n628\t\n629\t                    if !fallback_succeeded {\n630\t                        remaining_failed.insert(shard_id, error.clone());\n631\t                    }\n632\t                }\n633\t\n634\t                // Merge fallback results\n635\t                shard_pages.extend(fallback_pages);\n636\t\n637\t                // Update failed_shards with only those that truly failed\n638\t                if remaining_failed.is_empty() {\n639\t                    // All shards succeeded via fallback\n640\t                    return Ok(ScatterResult {\n641\t                        shard_pages,\n642\t                        failed_shards: HashMap::new(),\n643\t                        partial: false,\n644\t                        deadline_exceeded,\n645\t                    });\n646\t                } else {\n647\t                    // Some shards still failed\n648\t                    failed_shards = remaining_failed;\n649\t                }\n650\t            }\n651\t        }\n652\t    }\n653\t\n654\t    Ok(ScatterResult { shard_pages, failed_shards, partial, deadline_exceeded })\n655\t}\n656\t\n657\t#[instrument(skip_all, fields(index = %req.index_uid))]\n658\tpub async fn scatter_gather_search<C: NodeClient>(\n659\t    plan: ScatterPlan,\n660\t    client: &C,\n661\t    req: SearchRequest,\n662\t    topology: &Topology,\n663\t    policy: UnavailableShardPolicy,\n664\t    strategy: &dyn MergeStrategy,\n665\t) ->      body: serde_json::json!({\"success\": false, \"message\": format!(\"shard {} unavailable\", shard_id)}),\n673\t            });\n674\t        }\n675\t    }\n676\t\n677\t    // Collect failed shard shard_hits: shard_pages,\n682\t        offset: req.offset,\n683\t        limit: req.limit,\n684\t        client_requested_score: req.ranking_score,\n685\t        facets: req.facets.clone(),\n686\t ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n703\t\n704\t/// Extract unique query terms from a search query string.\n705\tpub fn extract_query_terms(query: = Vec::new();\n710\t            for term in q.split_whitespace() {\n711\t                let lower = term.to_lowercase();\n712\t                if seen.insert(lower.clone()) { terms.push(lower); \"a\", \"_rankingScore\": 0.9}], \"estimatedTotalHits\": 1, \"processingTimeMs\": 5}));\n1078\t        c.preflight_responses.insert(NodeId::new(\"node-0\".into()), PreflightResponse {\n1079\t            total_docs: 50000, avg_doc_length: 50.0,\n1080\t            term_stats: HashMap::from([(\"test\".into(), TermStats { df: 500 })]),\n1081\t        });\n1082\t        let s = assert!(!r.degraded);\n1085\t        assert!(!r.hits.is_empty());\n1086\t    }\n1087\t\n1088\t    /// Integration test for dfs_query_then_fetch with severely skewed shard distribution.\n1089\t    ///\n1090\t    /// This test simulates the scenario described in miroir-yio:\n1091\t    /// - Shard 0: Normal (1,000 docs, term df = 100)\n1092\t    /// - Shard 1: 100x normal (100,000 docs, term df = 10,000)\n1093\t    /// - Shard 2: Near-empty (10 docs, term df = 1)\n1094\t    ///\n1095\t    /// Without global IDF preflight, each shard would compute different local IDF values:\n1096\t    /// - Shard 0: IDF ≈ log((1000 - 100 + 0.5) / (100 + 0.5)) + 1 ≈ 2.3\n1097\t    /// - Shard 1: IDF ≈ log((100000 - 10000 + 0.5) / (10000 + 0.5)) + 1 ≈ 2.3\n1098\t    /// - Shard 2: IDF ≈ log((10 - 1 + 0.5) / (1 + 0.5)) + 1 ≈ 2.8\n1099\t    ///\n1100\t    /// With global IDF preflight, all shards use the same IDF:\n1101\t    /// - Global: N = 101,010, df = 10,101\n1102\t    /// - IDF ≈ log((101010 - 10101 + 0.5) / (10101 + 0.5)) + 1 ≈ 2.3\n1103\t    ///\n1104\t    /// This ensures scores are comparable across shards, enabling correct score-based merge.\n1105\t    #[tokio::test]\n1106\t    async fn test_dfs_skewed_shards_global_idf_aggregation() {\n1107\t        let mut topo = Topology::new(3, 1, 1);\n1108\t        topo.add_node(Node::new(NodeId::new(\"node-0\".into()), \"http://node-0:7700\".into(), 0));\n1109\t        topo.add_node(Node::new(NodeId::new(\"node-1\".into()), \"http://node-1:7700\".into(), 0));\n1110\t        topo.add_node(Node::new(NodeId::new(\"node-2\".into()), \"http://node-2:7700\".into(), 0));\n1111\t\n1112\t        let plan = plan_search_scatter(&topo, 0, 1, 3);\n1113\t\n1114\t        // Simulate severely skewed shard distribution\n1115\t        let mut c = MockNodeClient::default();\n1116\t\n1117\t        // Shard 0: Normal distribution\n1118\t        c.preflight_responses.insert(NodeId::new(\"node-0\".into()), PreflightResponse {\n1119\t            total_docs: 1000,\n1120\t            avg_doc_length: 50.0,\n1121\t            term_stats: HashMap::from([\n1122\t                (\"machine\".into(), TermStats { df: 100 }),\n1123\t                (\"learning\".into(), TermStats { df: 80 }),\n1124\t            ]),\n1125\t        });\n1126\t\n1127\t        // Shard 1: 100x normal (severely skewed)\n1128\t        c.preflight_responses.insert(NodeId::new(\"node-1\".into()), PreflightResponse {\n1129\t            total_docs: 100_000,\n1130\t            avg_doc_length: 55.0,\n1131\t            term_stats: HashMap::from([\n1132\t                (\"machine\".into(), TermStats { df: 10_000 }),\n1133\t                (\"learning\".into(), TermStats { df: 8_000 }),\n1134\t            ]),\n1135\t        });\n1136\t\n1137\t        // Shard 2: Near-empty\n1138\t        c.preflight_responses.insert(NodeId::new(\"node-2\".into()), PreflightResponse {\n1139\t            total_docs: 10,\n1140\t            avg_doc_length: 45.0,\n1141\t            term_stats: HashMap::from([\n1142\t                (\"machine\".into(), TermStats { df: 1 }),\n1143\t                (\"learning\".into(), TermStats { df: 1 }),\n1144\t            ]),\n1145\t        });\n1146\t\n1147\t        // Execute preflight to get global IDF\n1148\t        let preflight_req = PreflightRequest {\n1149\t            index_uid: \"test\".into(),\n1150\t            terms: vec![\"machine\".into(), \"learning\".into()],\n1151\t            filter: None,\n1152\t        };\n1153\t\n1154\t        let global_idf = execute_preflight(&plan, &c, &preflight_req, &topo).await.unwrap();\n1155\t\n1156\t        // Verify global aggregation\n1157\t        assert_eq!(global_idf.total_docs, 101_010);\n1158\t        assert_eq!(global_idf.terms.get(\"machine\").unwrap().df, 10_101);\n1159\t        assert_eq!(global_idf.terms.get(\"learning\").unwrap().df, 8_081);\n1160\t\n1161\t        // Verify global IDF is the same for all shards\n1162\t        // Expected IDF for \"machine\": log((101010 - 10101 + 0.5) / (10101 + 0.5)) + 1\n1163\t        let expected_idf_machine: f64 = ((101010.0_f64 - 10101.0 + 0.5) / (10101.0 + 0.5)).ln() + 1.0;\n1164\t        let actual_idf_machine = global_idf.terms.get(\"machine\").unwrap().idf;\n1165\t        assert!((actual_idf_machine - expected_idf_machine).abs() < 0.001);\n1166\t\n1167\t        // Expected IDF for \"learning\": log((101010 - 8081 + 0.5) / (8081 + 0.5)) + 1\n1168\t        let expected_idf_learning: f64 = ((101010.0_f64 - 8081.0 + 0.5) / (8081.0 + 0.5)).ln() + 1.0;\n1169\t        let actual_idf_learning = global_idf.terms.get(\"learning\").unwrap().idf;\n1170\t        assert!((actual_idf_learning - expected_idf_learning).abs() < 0.001);\n1171\t\n1172\t        // Verify that without global IDF, local IDF values would differ significantly\n1173\t        // Shard 0 local IDF for \"machine\": log((1000 - 100 + 0.5) / (100 + 0.5)) + 1 ≈ 3.19\n1174\t        // Shard 1 local IDF for \"machine\": log((100000 - 10000 + 0.5) / (10000 + 0.5)) + 1 ≈ 3.20\n1175\t        // Shard 2 local IDF for \"machine\": log((10 - 1 + 0.5) / (1 + 0.5)) + 1 ≈ 2.85\n1176\t        let local_idf_shard_0: f64 = ((1000.0_f64 - 100.0 + 0.5) / (100.0 + 0.5)).ln() + 1.0;\n1177\t        let local_idf_shard_2: f64 = ((10.0_f64 - 1.0 + 0.5) / (1.0 + 0.5)).ln() + 1.0;\n1178\t        assert!((local_idf_shard_2 - local_idf_shard_0).abs() > 0.2, \"Local IDF values should differ significantly\");\n1179\t        assert!((local_idf_shard_2 - actual_idf_machine).abs() > 0.3, \"Global IDF should be closer to large-shard local IDF\");\n1180\t    }\n1181\t\n1182\t    /// Test that DFS preflight handles empty query terms gracefully.\n1183\t    #[tokio::test]\n1184\t    async fn test_dfs_empty_query_terms() {\n1185\t        let topo = make_test_topology();\n1186\t        let plan = plan_search_scatter(&topo, 0, 2, 64);\n1187\t        let c = assert!(global_idf.terms.is_empty());\n1198\t    }\n1199\t\n1200\t    /// Test that DFS preflight handles partial failures gracefully.\n1201\t    #[tokio::test]\n1202\t    async fn mut total_docs = 0u64;\n        let mut total_length = 0.0f64;\n        let mut term_df: HashMap<String, u64> = HashMap::new();\n\n        for resp in responses {\n            total_docs += resp.total_docs;\n            total_length += resp.avg_doc_length * resp.total_docs as f64;\n            for (term, stats) in &resp.term_stats {\n                *term_df.entry(term.clone()).or_insert(0) += stats.df;\n            }\n        }\n\n        let avg_doc_length = if total_docs > 0 {\n            total_length / total_docs as f64\n        } else {\n            0.0\n        };\n\n        let n = total_docs as f64;\n        let terms = term_df\n            .into_iter()\n            .map(|(term, df)| {\n                let idf = if df == 0 {\n                    0.0\n                } else {\n                    ((n - df as f64 + 0.5) / (df as f64 + 0.5)).ln() + 1.0\n                };\n                (term, GlobalTermStats { df, idf })\n            })\n            .collect();\n\n        Self { total_docs, avg_doc_length, terms }\n    }\n}\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// NodeClient trait\n// Option<GlobalIdf>,\n}\n\nimpl SearchRequest {\n    /// Build the request body for sending to a node.\n    ///\n    /// Injects `showRankingScore: true` unconditionally so the merger can global-sort.\n    /// Each node receives `offset + limit` results to ensure the coordinator has enough\n    /// data to apply pagination.\n    pub fn to_node_body(&self) -> Value {\n        let mut body = self.body.clone();\n\n        // Inject showRankingScore: true unconditionally for global sorting\n        body[\"showRankingScore\"] = serde_json::json!(true);\n\n        // Set limit to offset + limit so we get enough results for pagination\n        // (coordinator applies final offset/limit after merging)\n        body[\"limit\"] = serde_json::json!(self.offset + self.limit);\n\n        // Set offset to 0 on individual nodes (coordinator handles offset)\n        body[\"offset\"] = serde_json::json!(0);\n\n        // Ensure query is set\n        if let Some(q) = &self.query {\n            body[\"q\"] = serde_json::json!(q);\n        }\n\n        // Ensure filter is set if provided\n        if let Some(filter) = &self.filter {\n            body[\"filter\"] = filter.clone();\n        }\n\n        // Ensure facets are set if provided\n        if let Some(facets) = &self.facets {\n            body[\"facets\"] = serde_json::json!(facets);\n        }\n\n        body\n    }\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug)]\npub struct ScatterResult {\n    pub shard_pages: Vec<ShardHitPage>,\n    pub failed_shards: HashMap<u32, NodeError>,\n    pub partial: bool,\n    pub deadline_exceeded: bool,\n}\n\n#[instrument(skip_all, fields(query_seq, rf, shard_count))]\npub fn plan_search_scatter(\n    topology: &Topology,\n    query_seq: u64,\n    rf: usize,\n    shard_count: u32,\n) -> ScatterPlan {\n    let chosen_group = query_group(query_seq, topology.replica_group_count());\n\n    let group = match topology.group(chosen_group) {\n        Some(g) => g,\n        None => {\n            return ScatterPlan {\n                chosen_group, target_shards: Vec::new(),\n                shard_to_node: HashMap::new(), deadline_ms: 0, hedging_eligible: false,\n            };\n        }\n    };\n\n    let _covering = covering_set(shard_count, group, rf, query_seq);\n\n    let mut shard_to_node = HashMap::new();\n    for shard_id in 0..shard_count {\n        let replicas = crate::router::assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, group.nodes(), rf);\n        let selected = replicas[(query_seq as usize) % replicas.len()].clone();\n        shard_to_node.insert(shard_id, selected);\n    }\n\n    ScatterPlan {\n        chosen_group,\n        target_shards: (0..shard_count).collect(),\n        shard_to_node,\n        deadline_ms: 5000,\n        hedging_eligible: group.node_count() > 1,\n    }\n}\n\n/// Plan search scatter with settings version floor filtering (plan §13.5).\n///\n/// Excludes nodes whose settings version for the given index is below `floor`.\n/// Returns None if no covering set can be assembled (caller should return 503).\npub fn plan_search_scatter_with_version_floor(\n    topology: &Topology,\n    query_seq: u64,\n    rf: usize,\n    shard_count: u32,\n    index: &str,\n    floor: u64,\n    version_checker: &impl Fn(&str, &str) -> u64,\n) -> Option<ScatterPlan> {\n    let chosen_group = query_group(query_seq, topology.replica_group_count());\n\n    let group = topology.group(chosen_group)?;\n\n    let covering = covering_set_with_version_floor(\n        shard_count,\n        group,\n        rf,\n        query_seq,\n        index,\n        floor,\n        version_checker,\n    )?;\n\n    let mut shard_to_node = HashMap::new();\n    for shard_id in 0..shard_count {\n        let replicas = crate::router::assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, group.nodes(), rf);\n        // Filter by version floor, then rotate by query_seq\n        let eligible: Vec<_> = replicas\n            .iter()\n            .filter(|node_id| {\n                let version = version_checker(index, node_id.as_str());\n                version >= floor\n            })\n            .collect();\n\n        if eligible.is_empty() {\n            return None;\n        }\n\n        let selected = eligible[query_seq as usize % eligible.len()];\n        shard_to_node.insert(shard_id, selected.clone());\n    }\n\n    Some(ScatterPlan {\n        chosen_group,\n        target_shards: (0..shard_count).collect(),\n        shard_to_node,\n        deadline_ms: 5000,\n        hedging_eligible: group.node_count() > 1,\n    })\n}\n\n/// Plan search scatter for a specific replica group (plan §13.6 session pinning).\n///\n/// Used when a session has a pending write and needs to read from the pinned group\n/// to ensure read-your-writes consistency.\npub fn plan_search_scatter_for_group(\n    topology: &Topology,\n    query_seq: u64,\n    rf: usize,\n    shard_count: u32,\n    pinned_group: u32,\n) -> Option<ScatterPlan> {\n    let group = topology.group(pinned_group)?;\n\n    let mut shard_to_node = HashMap::new();\n    for shard_id in 0..shard_count {\n        let replicas = crate::router::assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, group.nodes(), rf);\n        if replicas.is_empty() {\n            continue;\n        }\n        let selected = replicas[query_seq as usize % replicas.len()].clone();\n        shard_to_node.insert(shard_id, selected);\n    }\n\n    Some(ScatterPlan {\n        chosen_group: pinned_group,\n        target_shards: (0..shard_count).collect(),\n        shard_to_node,\n        deadline_ms: 5000,\n        hedging_eligible: group.node_count() > 1,\n    })\n}\n\n#[instrument(skip_all, fields(node_count))]\npub async fn execute_scatter<C: NodeClient>(\n    plan: ScatterPlan,\n    client: &C,\n    req: SearchRequest,\n    topology: &Topology,\n    policy: UnavailableShardPolicy,\n) -> Result<ScatterResult> {\n    let mut node_to_shards: HashMap<NodeId, Vec<u32>> = HashMap::new();\n    for (&shard_id, node_id) in &plan.shard_to_node {\n        if plan.target_shards.contains(&shard_id) {\n            node_to_shards.entry(node_id.clone()).or_default().push(shard_id);\n        }\n    }\n    tracing::Span::current().record(\"node_count\", node_to_shards.len());\n\n    let mut shard_pages = Vec::new();\n    let mut failed_shards = HashMap::new();\n    let mut deadline_exceeded = false;\n\n    let mut tasks = Vec::new();\n    for (node_id, shards) in node_to_shards {\n        let node = match topology.node(&node_id) {\n            Some(n) => n.clone(),\n            None => {\n                for shard_id in shards {\n                    failed_shards.insert(shard_id, NodeError::NetworkError(\"node not in topology\".to_string()));\n                }\n                continue;\n            }\n        };\n        let client_ref = client;\n        let req_clone = req.clone();\n        let node_id_clone = node_id.clone();\n        let shard_count = shards.len();\n        // Create a span for this node's scatter call\n        let span = info_span!(\n            \"scatter_node\",\n            node_id = %node_id_clone,\n            address = %node.address,\n            shard_count = shard_count,\n        );\n        tasks.push(async move {\n            let result = client_ref.search_node(&node_id_clone, &node.address, &req_clone).await;\n            (node_id_clone, shards, result)\n        }.instrument(span));\n    }\n\n    let results = futures_util::future::join_all(tasks).await;\n\n    for (_node_id, shards, result) in results {\n        match result {\n            Ok(body) => {\n                for _shard_id in shards {\n                    shard_pages.push(ShardHitPage { body: body.clone() });\n                }\n            }\n            Err(NodeError::Timeout) => {\n                deadline_exceeded = true;\n                for shard_id in shards { failed_shards.insert(shard_id, NodeError::Timeout); }\n            }\n            Err(e) => {\n                for shard_id in shards { failed_shards.insert(shard_id, e.clone()); }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    let partial = !failed_shards.is_empty();\n\n    match policy {\n        UnavailableShardPolicy::Error => {\n            if !failed_shards.is_empty() {\n                return Err(crate::error::MiroirError::Routing(format!(\"{} shard(s) unavailable\", failed_shards.len())));\n            }\n        }\n        UnavailableShardPolicy::Partial => {}\n        UnavailableShardPolicy::Fallback => {\n            // Group-unavailability fallback: try other replica groups for failed shards\n            if !failed_shards.is_empty() {\n                let mut fallback_pages = Vec::new();\n                let mut remaining_failed = HashMap::new();\n\n                for (&shard_id, error) in &failed_shards {\n                    let mut fallback_succeeded = false;\n\n                    // Try each other replica group\n                    for group_id in 0..topology.replica_group_count() {\n                        if group_id == plan.chosen_group {\n                            continue; // Skip the already-tried group\n                        }\n\n                        if let Some(group) = topology.group(group_id) {\n                            let replicas = crate::router::assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, group.nodes(), topology.rf());\n                            if replicas.is_empty() {\n                                continue;\n                            }\n\n                            // Try each replica in the fallback group\n                            for node_id in replicas {\n                                if let Some(node) = topology.node(&node_id) {\n                                    match client.search_node(&node_id, &node.address, &req).await {\n                                        Ok(body) => {\n                                            fallback_pages.push(ShardHitPage { body });\n                                            fallback_succeeded = true;\n                                            break;\n                                        }\n                                        Err(_) => {\n                                            continue; // Try next replica\n                                        }\n                                    }\n                                }\n                            }\n\n                            if fallback_succeeded {\n                                break; // Found a working replica\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n\n                    if !fallback_succeeded {\n                        remaining_failed.insert(shard_id, error.clone());\n                    }\n                }\n\n                // Merge fallback results\n                shard_pages.extend(fallback_pages);\n\n                // Update failed_shards with only those that truly failed\n                if remaining_failed.is_empty() {\n                    // All shards succeeded via fallback\n                    return Ok(ScatterResult {\n                        shard_pages,\n                        failed_shards: HashMap::new(),\n                        partial: false,\n                        deadline_exceeded,\n                    });\n                } else {\n                    // Some shards still failed\n                    failed_shards = remaining_failed;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    Ok(ScatterResult { shard_pages, failed_shards, partial, deadline_exceeded })\n}\n\n#[instrument(skip_all, fields(index = %req.index_uid))]\npub async fn scatter_gather_search<C: NodeClient>(\n    plan: ScatterPlan,\n    client: &C,\n    req: SearchRequest,\n    topology: &Topology,\n    policy: UnavailableShardPolicy,\n    strategy: &dyn MergeStrategy,\n) -> Result<MergedSearchResult> {\n    let scatter_result = execute_scatter(plan, client, req.clone(), topology, policy).await?;\n\n    let mut shard_pages = scatter_result.shard_pages;\n    if scatter_result.partial {\n        for shard_id in scatter_result.failed_shards.keys() {\n            shard_pages.push(ShardHitPage {\n                body: serde_json::json!({\"success\": false, \"message\": format!(\"shard {} unavailable\", shard_id)}),\n            });\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Collect failed shard IDs for the X-Miroir-Degraded header\n    let failed_shards: Vec<u32> = scatter_result.failed_shards.keys().copied().collect();\n\n    let merge_input = MergeInput {\n        shard_hits: shard_pages,\n        offset: req.offset,\n        limit: req.limit,\n        client_requested_score: req.ranking_score,\n        facets: req.facets.clone(),\n        failed_shards,\n    };\n\n    // Span for the merge operation\n    let _span = info_span!(\n        \"merge\",\n        shard_count = merge_input.shard_hits.len(),\n        offset = req.offset,\n        limit = req.limit,\n    ).entered();\n\n    strategy.merge(merge_input)\n}\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// OP#4: Global-IDF preflight execution\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n/// Extract unique query terms from a search query string.\npub fn extract_query_terms(query: &Option<String>) -> Vec<String> {\n    match query {\n        Some(q) if !q.is_empty() => {\n            let mut seen = std::collections::HashSet::new();\n            let mut terms = Vec::new();\n            for term in q.split_whitespace() {\n                let lower = term.to_lowercase();\n                if seen.insert(lower.clone()) { terms.push(lower); }\n            }\n            terms\n        }\n        _ => Vec::new(),\n    }\n}\n\n/// Execute the preflight phase: gather term frequencies from all shards.\n#[instrument(skip_all, fields(node_count, term_count = req.terms.len()))]\npub async fn execute_preflight<C: NodeClient>(\n    plan: &ScatterPlan,\n    client: &C,\n    req: &PreflightRequest,\n    topology: &Topology,\n) -> Result<GlobalIdf> {\n    if req.terms.is_empty() {\n        return Ok(GlobalIdf { total_docs: 0, avg_doc_length: 0.0, terms: HashMap::new() });\n    }\n\n    let mut node_to_shards: HashMap<NodeId, Vec<u32>> = HashMap::new();\n    for (&shard_id, node_id) in &plan.shard_to_node {\n        if plan.target_shards.contains(&shard_id) {\n            node_to_shards.entry(node_id.clone()).or_default().push(shard_id);\n        }\n    }\n\n    let mut tasks = Vec::new();\n    for (node_id, _) in node_to_shards {\n        let node = match topology.node(&node_id) {\n            Some(n) => n.clone(),\n            None => continue,\n        };\n        let client_ref = client;\n        let req_clone = req.clone();\n        let nid = node_id.clone();\n        tasks.push(async move { client_ref.preflight_node(&nid, &node.address, &req_clone).await });\n    }\n\n    let results = futures_util::future::join_all(tasks).await;\n    let responses: Vec<PreflightResponse> = results.into_iter().filter_map(|r| r.ok()).collect();\n    Ok(GlobalIdf::from_preflight_responses(&responses))\n}\n\n/// Execute a full dfs_query_then_fetch search (OP#4 global-IDF preflight).\n#[instrument(skip_all, fields(index = %req.index_uid))]\npub async fn dfs_query_then_fetch_search<C: NodeClient>(\n    plan: ScatterPlan,\n    client: &C,\n    req: SearchRequest,\n    topology: &Topology,\n    policy: UnavailableShardPolicy,\n    strategy: &dyn MergeStrategy,\n) -> Result<MergedSearchResult> {\n    let preflight_req = PreflightRequest {\n        index_uid: req.index_uid.clone(),\n        terms: extract_query_terms(&req.query),\n        filter: req.filter.clone(),\n    };\n    let global_idf = execute_preflight(&plan, client, &preflight_req, topology).await?;\n    let mut search_req = req;\n    search_req.global_idf = Some(global_idf);\n    scatter_gather_search(plan, client, search_req, topology, policy, strategy).await\n}\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Mock client\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default)]\npub struct MockNodeClient {\n    pub responses: HashMap<NodeId, Value>,\n    pub preflight_responses: HashMap<NodeId, PreflightResponse>,\n    pub write_responses: HashMap<NodeId, WriteResponse>,\n    pub fetch_responses: HashMap<NodeId, FetchDocumentsResponse>,\n    pub errors: HashMap<NodeId, NodeError>,\n    pub delay_ms: u64,\n}\n\nimpl NodeClient for MockNodeClient {\n    async fn search_node(\n        &self, node: &NodeId, _address: &str, _request: &SearchRequest,\n    ) -> std::result::Result<Value, NodeError> {\n        let _ = self.delay_ms;\n        if let Some(err) = self.errors.get(node) { return Err(err.clone()); }\n        Ok(self.responses.get(node).cloned().unwrap_or_else(|| {\n            serde_json::json!({\"hits\": [], \"estimatedTotalHits\": 0, \"processingTimeMs\": 0, \"facetDistribution\": {}})\n        }))\n    }\n\n    async fn preflight_node(\n        &self, node: &NodeId, _address: &str, _request: &PreflightRequest,\n    ) -> std::result::Result<PreflightResponse, NodeError> {\n        if let Some(err) = self.errors.get(node) { return Err(err.clone()); }\n        Ok(self.preflight_responses.get(node).cloned().unwrap_or_else(|| {\n            PreflightResponse { total_docs: 1000, avg_doc_length: 50.0, term_stats: HashMap::new() }\n        }))\n    }\n\n    async fn write_documents(\n        &self, node: &NodeId, _address: &str, _request: &WriteRequest,\n    ) -> std::result::Result<WriteResponse, NodeError> {\n        if let Some(err) = self.errors.get(node) { return Err(err.clone()); }\n        Ok(self.write_responses.get(node).cloned().unwrap_or_else(|| {\n            WriteResponse {\n                success: true,\n                task_uid: Some(1),\n                message: None,\n                code: None,\n                error_type: None,\n            }\n        }))\n    }\n\n    async fn delete_documents(\n        &self, node: &NodeId, _address: &str, _request: &DeleteByIdsRequest,\n    ) -> std::result::Result<DeleteResponse, NodeError> {\n        if let Some(err) = self.errors.get(node) { return Err(err.clone()); }\n        Ok(DeleteResponse {\n            success: true,\n            task_uid: Some(1),\n            message: None,\n            code: None,\n            error_type: None,\n        })\n    }\n\n    async fn delete_documents_by_filter(\n        &self, node: &NodeId, _address: &str, _request: &DeleteByFilterRequest,\n    ) -> std::result::Result<DeleteResponse, NodeError> {\n        if let Some(err) = self.errors.get(node) { return Err(err.clone()); }\n        Ok(DeleteResponse {\n            success: true,\n            task_uid: Some(1),\n            message: None,\n            code: None,\n            error_type: None,\n        })\n    }\n\n    async fn fetch_documents(\n        &self, node: &NodeId, _address: &str, request: &FetchDocumentsRequest,\n    ) -> std::result::Result<FetchDocumentsResponse, NodeError> {\n        if let Some(err) = self.errors.get(node) { return Err(err.clone()); }\n        // Return stored fetch response if available, otherwise return empty\n        let stored = self.fetch_responses.get(node).cloned().unwrap_or_else(|| {\n            FetchDocumentsResponse {\n                results: Vec::new(),\n                limit: request.limit,\n                offset: request.offset,\n                total: 0,\n            }\n        });\n\n        // Handle pagination: if offset exceeds total, return empty results\n        if request.offset as u64 >= stored.total {\n            return Ok(FetchDocumentsResponse {\n                results: Vec::new(),\n                limit: request.limit,\n                offset: request.offset,\n                total: stored.total,\n            });\n        }\n\n        Ok(stored)\n    }\n\n    fn get_task_status(\n        &self,\n        node: &NodeId,\n        _address: &str,\n        _request: &TaskStatusRequest,\n    ) -> impl std::future::Future<Output = std::result::Result<TaskStatusResponse, NodeError>> + Send {\n        let node = node.clone();\n        let task_uid = _request.task_uid;\n        let error = self.errors.get(&node).cloned();\n        async move {\n            if let Some(err) = error {\n                return Err(err);\n            }\n            Ok(TaskStatusResponse {\n                task_uid,\n                status: \"succeeded\".to_string(),\n                error: None,\n                error_type: None,\n            })\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n    use crate::topology::{Node, NodeId};\n\n    fn make_test_topology() -> Topology {\n test_global_idf_aggregation() {\n        let resp = vec![\n            PreflightResponse { total_docs: 50000, avg_doc_length: 50.0, term_stats: HashMap::from([(\"a\".into(), TermStats { df: 5000 })]) GlobalIdf::from_preflight_responses(&resp);\n        assert_eq!(g.total_docs, 100000);\n        assert!((g.avg_doc_length - 55.0).abs() < 0.001);\n        assert_eq!(g.terms.get(\"a\").unwrap().df,   }\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn test_execute_preflight() {\n        let topo = make_test_topology();\n        let plan = plan_search_scatter(&topo, 0, 2, 64);\n        let mut c = MockNodeClient::default();\n        c.preflight_responses.insert(NodeId::new(\"node-0\".into()), PreflightResponse {\n            total_docs: 30000, avg_doc_length: 50.0,\n            term_stats: HashMap::from([(\"search\".into(), TermStats { df: 3000 })]),\n        });\n        c.preflight_responses.insert(NodeId::new(\"node-1\".into()), PreflightResponse {\n            total_docs: 30000, avg_doc_length: 55.0,\n            term_stats: HashMap::from([(\"search\".into(), TermStats { df: 2500 })]),\n        });\n        c.preflight_responses.insert(NodeId::new(\"node-2\".into()), PreflightResponse {\n            total_docs: 40000, avg_doc_length: 52.0,\n            term_stats: HashMap::from([(\"search\".into(), TermStats { df: 4000 })]),\n        });\n        let req = assert_eq!(g.total_docs, 100000);\n        assert_eq!(g.terms.get(\"search\").unwrap().df, 9500);\n    }\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn test_dfs_query_then_fetch() {\n        let topo = make_test_topology();\n        let plan = plan_search_scatter(&topo, 0, 2, 64);\n        let mut c = MockNodeClient::default();\n        c.responses.insert(NodeId::new(\"node-0\".into()), serde_json::json!({\"hits\": [{\"id\": \"a\", \"_rankingScore\": 0.9}], \"estimatedTotalHits\": 1, \"processingTimeMs\": 5}));\n        c.preflight_responses.insert(NodeId::new(\"node-0\".into()), PreflightResponse {\n            total_docs: 50000, avg_doc_length: 50.0,\n            term_stats: HashMap::from([(\"test\".into(), TermStats { df: 500 })]),\n        });\n        let s = crate::merger::RrfStrategy::default_strategy();\n        let r = dfs_query_then_fetch_search(plan, &c, make_req(), &topo, UnavailableShardPolicy::Partial, &s).await.unwrap();\n        assert!(!r.degraded);\n        assert!(!r.hits.is_empty());\n    }\n\n    /// Integration test for dfs_query_then_fetch with severely skewed shard distribution.\n    ///\n    /// This test simulates the scenario described in miroir-yio:\n    /// - Shard 0: Normal (1,000 docs, term df = 100)\n    /// - Shard 1: 100x normal (100,000 docs, term df = 10,000)\n    /// - Shard 2: Near-empty (10 docs, term df = 1)\n    ///\n    /// Without global IDF preflight, each shard would compute different local IDF values:\n    /// - Shard 0: IDF ≈ log((1000 - 100 + 0.5) / (100 + 0.5)) + 1 ≈ 2.3\n    /// - Shard 1: IDF ≈ log((100000 - 10000 + 0.5) / (10000 + 0.5)) + 1 ≈ 2.3\n    /// - Shard 2: IDF ≈ log((10 - 1 + 0.5) / (1 + 0.5)) + 1 ≈ 2.8\n    ///\n    /// With global IDF preflight, all shards use the same IDF:\n    /// - Global: N = 101,010, df = 10,101\n    /// - IDF ≈ log((101010 - 10101 + 0.5) / (10101 + 0.5)) + 1 ≈ 2.3\n    ///\n    /// This ensures scores are comparable across shards, enabling correct score-based merge.\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn test_dfs_skewed_shards_global_idf_aggregation() {\n        let mut topo = Topology::new(3, 1, 1);\n        topo.add_node(Node::new(NodeId::new(\"node-0\".into()), \"http://node-0:7700\".into(), 0));\n        topo.add_node(Node::new(NodeId::new(\"node-1\".into()), \"http://node-1:7700\".into(), 0));\n        topo.add_node(Node::new(NodeId::new(\"node-2\".into()), \"http://node-2:7700\".into(), 0));\n\n        let plan = plan_search_scatter(&topo, 0, 1, 3);\n\n        // Simulate severely skewed shard distribution\n        let mut c = MockNodeClient::default();\n\n        // Shard 0: Normal distribution\n        c.preflight_responses.insert(NodeId::new(\"node-0\".into()), PreflightResponse {\n            total_docs: 1000,\n            avg_doc_length: 50.0,\n            term_stats: HashMap::from([\n                (\"machine\".into(), TermStats { df: 100 }),\n                (\"learning\".into(), TermStats { df: 80 }),\n            ]),\n        });\n\n        // Shard 1: 100x normal (severely skewed)\n        c.preflight_responses.insert(NodeId::new(\"node-1\".into()), PreflightResponse {\n            total_docs: 100_000,\n            avg_doc_length: 55.0,\n            term_stats: HashMap::from([\n                (\"machine\".into(), TermStats { df: 10_000 }),\n                (\"learning\".into(), TermStats { df: 8_000 }),\n            ]),\n        });\n\n        // Shard 2: Near-empty\n        c.preflight_responses.insert(NodeId::new(\"node-2\".into()), PreflightResponse {\n            total_docs: 10,\n            avg_doc_length: 45.0,\n            term_stats: HashMap::from([\n                (\"machine\".into(), TermStats { df: 1 }),\n                (\"learning\".into(), TermStats { df: 1 }),\n            ]),\n        });\n\n        // Execute preflight to get global IDF\n        let preflight_req = PreflightRequest {\n            index_uid: \"test\".into(),\n            terms: vec![\"machine\".into(), \"learning\".into()],\n            filter: None,\n        };\n\n        let global_idf = execute_preflight(&plan, &c, &preflight_req, &topo).await.unwrap();\n\n        // Verify global aggregation\n        assert_eq!(global_idf.total_docs, 101_010);\n        assert_eq!(global_idf.terms.get(\"machine\").unwrap().df, 10_101);\n        assert_eq!(global_idf.terms.get(\"learning\").unwrap().df, 8_081);\n\n        // Verify global IDF is the same for all shards\n        // Expected IDF for \"machine\": log((101010 - 10101 + 0.5) / (10101 + 0.5)) + 1\n        let expected_idf_machine: f64 = ((101010.0_f64 - 10101.0 + 0.5) / (10101.0 + 0.5)).ln() + 1.0;\n        let actual_idf_machine = global_idf.terms.get(\"machine\").unwrap().idf;\n        assert!((actual_idf_machine - expected_idf_machine).abs() < 0.001);\n\n        // Expected IDF for \"learning\": log((101010 - 8081 + 0.5) / /// - Active/Draining → Failed (health check detects failure)\n70\t    /// - Failed → Active          (health check recovery)\n71\t    /// - Active/Failed → Degraded (partial health: timeouts)\n72\t    /// - Degraded → Active        (health restored)\n73\t    pub fn transition_to(self, target: NodeStatus) -> Result<NodeStatus> {\n74\t        use NodeStatus::*;\n75\t\n76\t        let legal = match (self, target) {\n77\t            // Normal lifecycle\n78\t            (Joining, Active) => true,\n79\t            (Active, Draining) => true,\n80\t            (Draining, Removed) => true,\n81\t\n82\t            // Failure detection\n83\t            (Active, Failed) => true,\n84\t            (Draining, Failed) => true,\n85\t\n86\t            // Recovery\n87\t            (Failed, Active) => true,\n88\t\n89\t            // Degraded\n90\t            (Active, Degraded) => true,\n91\t            (Failed, Degraded) => true,\n92\t            (Degraded, Active) => true,\n93\t\n94\t            // Idempotent\n95\t            (Active, Active)\n96\t            | (Failed, Failed)\n97\t            | (Degraded, Degraded)\n98\t            | (Joining, Joining)\n99\t            | (Draining, Draining) => true,\n100\t\n101\t            // Healthy is an alias for Active in transitions\n102\t            (Healthy, _) | (_, Healthy) => false,\n103\t\n104\t            _ => false,\n105\t        };\n106\t\n107\t        if legal {\n108\t            Ok(target)\n109\t        } else {\n110\t            Err(MiroirError::Topology(format!(\n111\t                \"illegal state transition: {:?} → self.node_index.insert(node.id.clone(), idx);\n300\t        let group_id = node.replica_group;\n301\t        self.nodes.push(node);\n302\t        self.rebuild_groups();\n303\t        self.replica_groups = self.replica_groups.max(group_id + 1);\n304\t    }\n305\t\n306\t    /// Get a node by ID.\n307\t    pub fn node(&self, id: &NodeId) -> Option<&Node> {\n308\t        self.node_index.get(id).map(|&i| &self.nodes[i])\n309\t    }\n310\t\n311\t    /// Get a mutable node by ID.\n312\t    pub fn node_mut(&mut self, id: &NodeId) -> Option<&mut Node> {\n313\t        self.node_index.get(id).copied().map(move |i| &mut self.nodes[i])\n314\t    }\n315\t\n316\t    /// Iterate over all nodes.\n317\t    pub fn nodes(&self) -> impl Iterator<Item = &Node> {\n318\t        self.nodes.iter()\n319\t    }\n320\t\n321\t    /// Get a group by ID.\n322\t    pub fn group(&self, id: u32) -> Option<&Group> {\n323\t        self.groups.get(id as usize)\n324\t    }\n325\t\n326\t    /// Iterate over all groups in ascending order by ID.\n327\t    pub fn groups(&self) -> impl Iterator<Item = &Group> {\n328\t        self.groups.iter()\n329\t    }\n330\t\n331\t    /// Get the replication factor.\n332\t    pub fn rf(&self) -> usize {\n333\t        self.rf\n334\t    }\n335\t\n336\t    /// Get the number of replica groups.\n337\t    pub fn replica_group_count(&self) -> u32 {\n338\t        self.groups.len() as u32\n339\t    }\n340\t\n341\t    /// Build a HashMap<NodeId, Node> for use with Group::healthy_nodes.\n342\t    pub fn node_map(&self) -> HashMap<NodeId, Node> {\n343\t        self.nodes.iter().map(|n| (n.id.clone(), n.clone())).collect()\n344\t    }\n345\t\n346\t    /// Remove a node from the topology.\n347\t    pub fn remove_node(&mut self, id: &NodeId) -> bool {\n348\t        if let Some(&idx) = self.node_index.get(id) {\n349\t            self.node_index.remove(id);\n350\t            self.nodes.remove(idx);\n351\t            // Rebuild indices\n352\t            self.node_index.clear();\n353\t            for (i, node) in self.nodes.iter().enumerate() {\n354\t                self.node_index.insert(node.id.clone(), i);\n355\t            }\n356\t            self.rebuild_groups();\n357\t            true\n358\t        } else {\n359\t            false\n360\t        }\n361\t    }\n362\t\n363\t    /// Remove all nodes in a replica group and the group itself.\n364\t    pub fn remove_group(&mut self, group_id: u32) -> bool {\n365\t        // Find all nodes in this group\n366\t        let nodes_to_remove: Vec<NodeId> = self\n367\t            .nodes\n368\t            .iter()\n369\t            .filter(|n| n.replica_group == group_id)\n370\t            .map(|n| n.id.clone())\n371\t            .collect();\n372\t\n373\t        if nodes_to_remove.is_empty() {\n374\t            return false;\n375\t        }\n376\t\n377\t        // Remove all nodes in the group\n378\t        for node_id in nodes_to_remove {\n379\t            self.remove_node(&node_id);\n380\t        }\n381\t\n382\t        true\n383\t    }\n384\t\n385\t    fn rebuild_groups(&mut self) {\n386\t        let num_groups = self\n387\t            .nodes\n388\t            .iter()\n389\t            .map(|n| n.replica_group)\n390\t            .max()\n391\t            .map_or(self.replica_groups as usize, |m| (m as usize + 1).max(self.replica_groups as usize));\n392\t\n393\t        self.groups = (0..num_groups).map(|i| Group::new(i as u32)).collect();\n394\t        for node in &self.nodes {\n395\t            if let Some(group) = self.groups.get_mut(node.replica_group as usize) {\n396\t                group.add_node(node.id.clone());\n397\t            }\n398\t        }\n399\t    }\n400\t}\n401\t\n402\timpl Serialize for Topology {\n403\t    fn serialize<S: Serializer>(&self, serializer: S) -> std::result::Result<S::Ok, S::Error> {\n404\t        #[derive(Serialize)]\n405\t        struct TopologyData {\n406\t            shards: u32,\n407\t            replica_groups: u32,\n408\t            rf: usize,\n409\t            nodes: Vec<Node>,\n410\t        }\n411\t        TopologyData {\n412\t            shards: self.shards,\n413\t            replica_groups: self.replica_groups,\n414\t            rf: self.rf,\n415\t            nodes: self.nodes.clone(),\n416\t        }\n417\t        .serialize(serializer)\n418\t    }\n419\t}\n420\t\n421\timpl<'de> Deserialize<'de> for Topology {\n422\t    fn deserialize<D: Deserializer<'de>>(deserializer: D) -> std::result::Result<Self, D::Error> {\n423\t        #[derive(Deserialize)]\n424\t        struct TopologyData {\n425\t            shards: u32,\n426\t            #[serde(default)]\n427\t            replica_groups: u32,\n428\t            #[serde(alias = \"replication_factor\", default)]\n429\t            rf: usize,\n430\t            #[serde(default)]\n431\t            nodes: Vec<Node>,\n432\t        }\n433\t\n434\t        let data = TopologyData::deserialize(deserializer)?;\n435\t        let mut topo = Self {\n436\t            shards: data.shards,\n437\t            replica_groups: data.replica_groups,\n438\t            rf: data.rf,\n439\t            nodes: data.nodes,\n440\t            groups: Vec::new(),\n441\t            node_index: HashMap::new(),\n442\t        };\n443\t        // Build lookup index\n444\t        for (i, node) in topo.nodes.iter().enumerate() {\n445\t            topo.node_index.insert(node.id.clone(), i);\n446\t        }\n447\t        // Derive replica_groups from nodes if not set\n448\t        if topo.replica_groups == 0 && !topo.nodes.is_empty() {\n449\t            topo.replica_groups = topo.nodes.iter().map(|n| n.replica_group).max().unwrap() + 1;\n450\t        }\n451\t        topo.rebuild_groups();\n452\t        Ok(topo)\n453\t    }\n454\t}\n455\t\n456\t#[cfg(test)]\n457\tmod tests {\n458\t    use super::*;\n459\t\n460\t    // ── YAML deserialization {\n576\t        use NodeStatus::*;\n577\t\n578\t        let cases: Vec<(NodeStatus, NodeStatus)> = vec![\n579\t            (Joining, Active),\n580\t            (Active, Draining),\n581\t            (Draining, Removed),\n582\t            (Active, Failed),\n583\t            (Draining, Failed),\n584\t            (Failed, Active),\n585\t            (Active, Degraded),\n586\t            (Failed, Degraded),\n587\t            (Degraded, Active),\n588\t            // Idempotent\n589\t            (Active, Active),\n590\t            (Failed, Failed),\n591\t            (Degraded, Degraded),\n592\t            (Joining, Joining),\n593\t            (Draining, Draining),\n594\t        ];\n595\t\n596\t        for (from, to) in cases {\n597\t            assert!(\n598\t                from.transition_to(to).is_ok(),\n599\t                \"expected {:?} → {:?} to succeed\",\n600\t                from,\n601\t                to\n602\t            );\n603\t        }\n604\t    }\n605\t\n606\t    #[test]\n607\t    fn illegal_transitions() {\n608\t        use NodeStatus::*;\n609\t\n610\t        let cases: Vec<(NodeStatus, NodeStatus)> = vec![\n611\t            // Skip steps\n612\t            (Joining, Draining),\n613\t            (Joining, Failed),\n614\t            (Joining, Removed),\n615\t            (Joining, Degraded),\n616\t            // Can't go back from Draining to Active\n617\t            (Draining, Active),\n618\t            (Draining, Joining),\n619\t            // Can't recover to Joining\n620\t            (Active, Joining),\n621\t            (Failed, Joining),\n622\t            (Degraded, Joining),\n623\t            // Removed is terminal\n624\t            (Removed, Active),\n625\t            (Removed, Joining),\n626\t            (Removed, Failed),\n627\t            (Removed, Degraded),\n628\t            (Removed, Draining),\n629\t            // Healthy not used in transitions\n630\t            (Healthy, Active),\n631\t            (Active, Healthy),\n632\t            // More illegal paths\n633\t            (Failed, Draining),\n634\t            (Failed, Removed),\n635\t            (Degraded, Failed),\n636\t            (Degraded, Draining),\n637\t            (Degraded, Removed),\n638\t        ];\n639\t\n640\t        for (from, to) in cases {\n641\t            let result = from.transition_to(to);\n642\t            assert!(\n643\t                result.is_err(),\n644\t                \"expected {:?} → {:?} to be rejected, but got Ok({:?})\",\n645\t                from,\n646\t                to,\n647\t                result.unwrap()\n648\t            );\n649\t        }\n650\t    }\n651\t\n652\t    #[test]\n653\t    fn node_transition_method() {\n654\t        let mut node = Node::new(\n655\t            NodeId::new(\"n0\".into()),\n656\t            \"http://n0:7700\".into(),\n657\t            0,\n658\t        );\n659\t        assert_eq!(node.status, NodeStatus::Joining);\n660\t\n661\t
